2011A01660 T00017       AN ACT to amend the environmental conservation law, in relation to regu-
2011A01660 T00018         lating perchloroethylene dry cleaning facilities
2011A01660 T00019
2011A01660 T00020         THE PEOPLE OF THE STATE OF NEW YORK, REPRESENTED IN SENATE AND  ASSEM-
2011A01660 T00021       BLY, DO ENACT AS FOLLOWS:
2011A01660 T00022
2011A01660 T00023    1    Section 1. Article 19 of the environmental conservation law is amended
2011A01660 T00024    2  by adding a new title 13 to read as follows:
2011A01660 T00025    3                                  TITLE 13
2011A01660 T00026    4                  PERCHLOROETHYLENE DRY CLEANING FACILITIES
2011A01660 T00027    5  SECTION 19-1301. DEFINITIONS.
2011A01660 T00028    6          19-1303. VARIANCES.
2011A01660 T00029    7          19-1305. PROHIBITIONS.
2011A01660 T00030    8          19-1307. PRE-PERMITTING REQUIREMENTS FOR EXISTING FACILITIES.
2011A01660 T00031    9          19-1309. EQUIPMENT STANDARDS AND SPECIFICATIONS.
2011A01660 T00032   10          19-1311. LEAK INSPECTION AND SELF MONITORING REQUIREMENTS.
2011A01660 T00033   11          19-1313. OPERATION AND MAINTENANCE REQUIREMENTS.
2011A01660 T00034   12          19-1315. PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER MANAGEMENT.
2011A01660 T00035   13          19-1317. HAZARDOUS WASTE MANAGEMENT.
2011A01660 T00036   14          19-1319. EMERGENCY RESPONSE.
2011A01660 T00037   15          19-1321. REPORTING AND RECORDKEEPING.
2011A01660 T00038   16          19-1323. EQUIPMENT TESTING AND CERTIFICATION.
2011A01660 T00039   17          19-1325.  DRY  CLEANING  OWNER/MANAGER,  OPERATOR  AND INSPECTOR
2011A01660 T00040   18                     TRAINING AND CERTIFICATION.
2011A01660 T00041   19          19-1327. PERMITTING.

2011A01660 T00046   24  S 19-1301. DEFINITIONS.
2011A01660 T00047   25    FOR THE PURPOSE OF THIS TITLE, THE FOLLOWING DEFINITIONS SHALL APPLY:

2011A01660 T00054
2011A01660 T00055    1    (1) ADSORPTIVE CARTRIDGE FILTER. A REPLACEABLE CARTRIDGE  FILTER  THAT
2011A01660 T00056    2  CONTAINS DIATOMACEOUS EARTH OR ACTIVATED CLAY AS THE FILTER MEDIUM.
2011A01660 T00057    3    (2)  ANCILLARY  EQUIPMENT.  THE  EQUIPMENT  USED  WITH  A DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T00058    4  MACHINE IN A DRY CLEANING SYSTEM INCLUDING, BUT NOT LIMITED TO, EMISSION
2011A01660 T00059    5  CONTROL DEVICES, PUMPS, FILTERS, MUCK COOKERS,  STILLS,  SOLVENT  TANKS,
2011A01660 T00060    6  SOLVENT  CONTAINERS, WATER SEPARATORS, EXHAUST DAMPERS, DIVERTER VALVES,
2011A01660 T00061    7  INTERCONNECTING PIPING, HOSES AND DUCTS.
2011A01660 T00062    8    (3) ARTICLES. CLOTHING, GARMENTS, TEXTILES,  FABRICS,  LEATHER  GOODS,
2011A01660 T00063    9  AND THE LIKE, THAT ARE DRY CLEANED.
2011A01660 T00064   10    (4)  AZEOTROPIC  CONTROL  DEVICE.  A DRY CLEANING CONTROL SYSTEM WHERE
2011A01660 T00065   11  PERC EMISSIONS FROM THE  DRY  CLEANING  MACHINE  ARE  FIRST  COOLED  AND
2011A01660 T00066   12  CONDENSED, AND ARE THEN TREATED WITH WATER TO FURTHER DISPLACE PERC FROM
2011A01660 T00067   13  THE  ARTICLES  UPON  BEING RETURNED TO THE DRYER, CONDENSER, AND SOLVENT
2011A01660 T00068   14  STORAGE TANK. THERE IS NO EXHAUST TO THE ATMOSPHERE  DURING  THE  DRYING
2011A01660 T00069   15  CYCLE.
2011A01660 T00070   16    (5)  CARBON ADSORBER. AN AIR CLEANING DEVICE THAT CONSISTS OF AN INLET
2011A01660 T00071   17  FOR EXHAUST GASES FROM A DRY CLEANING MACHINE; ACTIVATED CARBON  IN  THE
2011A01660 T00072   18  FORM  OF A FIXED BED, CARTRIDGE, OR CANISTER, AS AN ADSORBENT; AN OUTLET
2011A01660 T00073   19  FOR EXHAUST GASES; AND A SYSTEM  TO  REGENERATE,  OR  RECLAIM  SATURATED
2011A01660 T00074   20  ADSORBENT.
2011A01660 T00075   21    (6) CARTRIDGE FILTER. A REPLACEABLE CARTRIDGE FILTER THAT CONTAINS ONE
2011A01660 T00076   22  OF THE FOLLOWING AS THE FILTER MEDIUM: PAPER, ACTIVATED CARBON, OR PAPER
2011A01660 T00077   23  AND  ACTIVATED CARBON. A CARTRIDGE FILTER CONTAINS NO DIATOMACEOUS EARTH
2011A01660 T00078   24  OR ACTIVATED CLAY. CARTRIDGE FILTERS INCLUDE, BUT ARE  NOT  LIMITED  TO:
2011A01660 T00079   25  STANDARD  FILTER, SPLIT FILTERS, "JUMBO" FILTERS, AND ALL CARBON POLISH-
2011A01660 T00080   26  ING FILTERS.
2011A01660 T00081   27    (7) CLOSED-LOOP MACHINE. DRY  CLEANING  EQUIPMENT  IN  WHICH  WASHING,
2011A01660 T00082   28  EXTRACTION,  AND  DRYING ARE ALL PERFORMED IN THE SAME SINGLE UNIT (ALSO
2011A01660 T00083   29  KNOWN AS A DRY-TO-DRY UNIT)  AND  WHICH  RECIRCULATES  PERC-LADEN  VAPOR
2011A01660 T00084   30  THROUGH  A  PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEM (E.G. REFRIGERATED CONDENSER) WITH NO
2011A01660 T00085   31  EXHAUST TO THE ATMOSPHERE DURING THE DRYING CYCLE. A CLOSED-LOOP MACHINE
2011A01660 T00086   32  MAY ALLOW FOR VENTING TO THE AMBIENT AIR THROUGH A LOCAL EXHAUST  VENTI-
2011A01660 T00087   33  LATION  SYSTEM,  SUCH  AS A DOOR FAN, AFTER THE DRYING CYCLE IS COMPLETE
2011A01660 T00088   34  AND ONLY WHILE THE MACHINE DOOR IS OPEN.
2011A01660 T00089   35    (8) CO-LOCATED. SHARING A COMMON WALL, FLOOR, OR CEILING WITH A  RESI-
2011A01660 T00090   36  DENCE OR BUSINESS.
2011A01660 T00091   37    (9)  COLORIMETRIC  DETECTOR  TUBE. A GLASS TUBE (SEALED PRIOR TO USE),
2011A01660 T00092   38  CONTAINING MATERIAL IMPREGNATED WITH A CHEMICAL  THAT  IS  SENSITIVE  TO
2011A01660 T00093   39  PERC AND IS DESIGNED TO MEASURE THE CONCENTRATION OF PERC IN AIR.
2011A01660 T00094   40    (10)  COMMERCIAL BUILDING. ANY BUILDING WHERE ONLY COMMERCIAL BUSINESS
2011A01660 T00095   41  IS CONDUCTED, SUCH AS AN OFFICE BUILDING OR STRIP MALL.
2011A01660 T00096   42    (11) CONDENSER. AN AIR CLEANING DEVICE THAT REMOVES CONDENSABLE VAPORS
2011A01660 T00097   43  BY A REDUCTION IN THE TEMPERATURE OF THE EXHAUST GASES OR, IN  THE  CASE
2011A01660 T00098   44  OF  A SURFACE CONDENSER, BY CONTACT OF THE EXHAUST GASES WITH STRUCTURES
2011A01660 T00099   45  THAT ARE COOLED BY A CIRCULATING COOLING FLUID.
2011A01660 T00000.SO DOC A 1660                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01660 T00100   46    (12) CONVERTED MACHINE. AN EXISTING VENTED MACHINE THAT HAS BEEN MODI-
2011A01660 T00101   47  FIED TO BE A CLOSED-LOOP  MACHINE  BY  ELIMINATING  THE  AERATION  STEP,
2011A01660 T00102   48  INSTALLING  A PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEM, AND PROVIDING FOR RECIRCULATION OF
2011A01660 T00103   49  THE PERC-LADEN VAPOR WITH NO  EXHAUST  TO  THE  ATMOSPHERE  OR  WORKROOM
2011A01660 T00104   50  DURING  THE  DRYING  CYCLE. A CONVERTED MACHINE MAY ALLOW FOR VENTING TO
2011A01660 T00105   51  THE AMBIENT AIR THROUGH A LOCAL EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEM,  SUCH  AS  A
2011A01660 T00106   52  DOOR  FAN, AFTER THE DRYING CYCLE IS COMPLETE AND ONLY WHILE THE MACHINE
2011A01660 T00107   53  DOOR IS OPEN.
2011A01660 T00108   54    (13) COOL-DOWN. THE PORTION OF THE DRYING CYCLE THAT BEGINS  WHEN  THE
2011A01660 T00109   55  HEATING  MECHANISM  DEACTIVATES AND THE REFRIGERATED CONDENSER CONTINUES
2011A01660 T00110
2011A01660 T00111       A. 1660                             3
2011A01660 T00112
2011A01660 T00113    1  TO REDUCE THE TEMPERATURE OF THE AIR RECIRCULATING THROUGH THE  DRUM  TO
2011A01660 T00114    2  REDUCE THE CONCENTRATION OF PERC IN THE DRUM.
2011A01660 T00115    3    (14) DESORPTION. REGENERATION OR STRIPPING OF AN ACTIVATED CARBON BED,
2011A01660 T00116    4  OR  ANY  OTHER TYPE OF VAPOR ADSORBER BY REMOVAL OF THE ADSORBED SOLVENT
2011A01660 T00117    5  USING HOT AIR, STEAM, OR OTHER MEANS.
2011A01660 T00118    6    (15) DIP TANK. A SEPARATE TANK THAT CONTAINS  PERC  AND  IS  USED  FOR
2011A01660 T00119    7  PURPOSES OTHER THAN DRY CLEANING (E.G. WATERPROOFING).
2011A01660 T00120    8    (16) DIVERTER VALVE. A FLOW CONTROL DEVICE THAT PREVENTS ROOM AIR FROM
2011A01660 T00121    9  PASSING THROUGH A REFRIGERATED CONDENSER WHEN THE DOOR OF A DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T00122   10  MACHINE IS OPEN.
2011A01660 T00123   11    (17)  DOOR FAN. A LOCAL EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEM DESIGNED TO PROVIDE
2011A01660 T00124   12  FOR A MINIMUM 100 FPM INWARD AIR VELOCITY OR EQUIVALENT INTO THE  EFFEC-
2011A01660 T00125   13  TIVE  DOOR  OPEN  AREA  OF  A  DRY CLEANING MACHINE WHENEVER THE DOOR IS
2011A01660 T00126   14  OPENED, AND WHERE THE PERC EMISSIONS ARE CONTROLLED BY A CARBON ADSORBER
2011A01660 T00127   15  OR EQUIVALENT CONTROL PRIOR TO VENTING TO THE OUTER AIR.
2011A01660 T00128   16    (18) DRUM. THE ROTATING CYLINDER OR WHEEL OF THE DRY CLEANING  MACHINE
2011A01660 T00129   17  THAT HOLDS THE ARTICLES BEING CLEANED.
2011A01660 T00130   18    (19)  DRY  CLEANING.  THE PROCESS USED TO REMOVE SOIL, GREASES, PAINTS
2011A01660 T00131   19  AND OTHER UNWANTED SUBSTANCES FROM ARTICLES WITH THE USE OF PERC.
2011A01660 T00132   20    (20) DRY CLEANING CONTROL SYSTEM.  EQUIPMENT  (E.G.  CARBON  ADSORBER,
2011A01660 T00133   21  REFRIGERATED CONDENSER, AZEOTROPIC UNIT, ETC.) OR AN AIR CLEANING DEVICE
2011A01660 T00134   22  USED  TO REDUCE THE AMOUNT OF AIR POLLUTANT(S) IN AN AIR STREAM PRIOR TO
2011A01660 T00135   23  DISCHARGE TO THE ATMOSPHERE.
2011A01660 T00136   24    (21) DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT. ANY MACHINE, DEVICE, OR APPARATUS USED TO
2011A01660 T00137   25  DRY CLEAN ARTICLES.
2011A01660 T00138   26    (22) DRY CLEANING FACILITY. AN ESTABLISHMENT  WITH  ONE  OR  MORE  DRY
2011A01660 T00139   27  CLEANING SYSTEMS.
2011A01660 T00140   28    (23)  DRY CLEANING SYSTEM. ALL OF THE FOLLOWING EQUIPMENT, DEVICES, OR
2011A01660 T00141   29  APPARATUS ASSOCIATED WITH THE PERC DRY CLEANING  OPERATIONS,  INCLUDING,
2011A01660 T00142   30  BUT  NOT  LIMITED  TO:  DRY  CLEANING  EQUIPMENT; FILTER OR PURIFICATION
2011A01660 T00143   31  SYSTEMS; WASTE HOLDING, TREATMENT,  OR  DISPOSAL  SYSTEMS;  PERC  SUPPLY
2011A01660 T00144   32  SYSTEMS;  DIP  TANKS; PUMPS; GASKETS; PIPING, DUCTING, FITTINGS, VALVES,
2011A01660 T00145   33  OR FLANGES THAT CONVEY PERC-CONTAMINATED AIR; AND DRY  CLEANING  CONTROL
2011A01660 T00146   34  SYSTEMS.
2011A01660 T00147   35    (24)  DRYING  CABINET.  A  HOUSING  IN  WHICH MATERIALS THAT HAVE BEEN
2011A01660 T00148   36  PREVIOUSLY DRY CLEANED IN PERC ARE  DRIED  INSTEAD  OF  BEING  DRIED  BY
2011A01660 T00149   37  TUMBLING IN A DRY CLEANING MACHINE.
2011A01660 T00150   38    (25)  DRYING  CYCLE.  THE  OPERATION  USED TO ACTIVELY REMOVE THE PERC
2011A01660 T00151   39  REMAINING IN THE MATERIALS AFTER WASHING AND EXTRACTION. FOR CLOSED-LOOP
2011A01660 T00152   40  MACHINES, THE HEATED PORTION OF THE CYCLE IS FOLLOWED BY  COOL-DOWN  AND
2011A01660 T00153   41  MAY  BE EXTENDED BEYOND COOL-DOWN BY THE ACTIVATION OF A CONTROL SYSTEM.
2011A01660 T00154   42  THE DRYING CYCLE BEGINS WHEN HEATING COILS ARE ACTIVATED AND  ENDS  WHEN
2011A01660 T00155   43  THE MACHINE CEASES ROTATION OF THE DRUM.
2011A01660 T00156   44    (26)  DRYING  SENSOR. A DEVICE THAT SENSES WHEN ARTICLES BEING CLEANED
2011A01660 T00157   45  ARE RELATIVELY DRY AND AUTOMATICALLY CONTROLS THE DRYING CYCLE.   DRYING
2011A01660 T00158   46  SENSORS  INCLUDE  BUT  ARE  NOT  LIMITED  TO:  INFRARED ANALYZERS, FLOAT
2011A01660 T00159   47  SWITCHES, AND RESISTANCE PROBES. THE DEVICE DETECTS THE CONCENTRATION OF
2011A01660 T00160   48  SYNTHETIC SOLVENTS IN THE DRYING AIR OR THAT THE LIQUID SOLVENT RECOVERY
2011A01660 T00161   49  RATE IS AT A MINIMAL RATE. THE DRYING SENSOR EXTENDS  THE  DRYING  CYCLE
2011A01660 T00162   50  FOR A MINIMUM TIME BEYOND THE ACTIVATION POINT TO DRY ARTICLES.
2011A01660 T00163   51    (27) DRY-TO-DRY MACHINE. A ONE-MACHINE DRY CLEANING OPERATION IN WHICH
2011A01660 T00164   52  DRYING AND WASHING ARE PERFORMED IN THE SAME MACHINE.
2011A01660 T00165   53    (28)  DRY-TO-DRY VENTED MACHINE. DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT IN WHICH WASH-
2011A01660 T00166   54  ING, EXTRACTION, AND DRYING ARE ALL PERFORMED IN THE  SAME  SINGLE  UNIT
2011A01660 T00167   55  AND  IN  WHICH FRESH AIR IS INTRODUCED INTO THE DRUM IN THE LAST STEP OF
2011A01660 T00168
2011A01660 T00169       A. 1660                             4
2011A01660 T00170
2011A01660 T00171    1  THE DRYING CYCLE AND EXHAUSTED TO THE OUTDOOR ATMOSPHERE, EITHER DIRECT-
2011A01660 T00172    2  LY OR THROUGH A CONTROL DEVICE (2ND GENERATION EQUIPMENT).
2011A01660 T00173    3    (29)  ENVIRONMENTAL TRAINING PROGRAM. AN INITIAL COURSE OR A REFRESHER
2011A01660 T00174    4  COURSE OF THE ENVIRONMENTAL TRAINING PROGRAM, FOR OWNERS  AND  OPERATORS
2011A01660 T00175    5  OF  PERC DRY CLEANING OPERATIONS THAT HAS BEEN AUTHORIZED BY THE DEPART-
2011A01660 T00176    6  MENT.
2011A01660 T00177    7    (30) EQUIVALENT CLOSED-LOOP VAPOR RECOVERY SYSTEM. A DEVICE OR  COMBI-

2011A01660 T00179    9  ANCE EQUAL TO OR EXCEEDING THAT OF REFRIGERATED CONDENSERS.

2011A01660 T00181   11  OR  AT  WHICH DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT WAS OPERATED PRIOR TO THE EFFECTIVE
2011A01660 T00182   12  DATE OF THIS TITLE.

2011A01660 T00184   14  BUILDINGS  LOCATED,  OWNED BY ONE PERSON, AND LOCATED ON THE SAME PARCEL
2011A01660 T00185   15  OR CONTIGUOUS PARCELS, IN WHICH PERC DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT IS  OPERATED
2011A01660 T00186   16  OR SET UP TO OPERATE.

2011A01660 T00188   18  EARTH, WHICH MUST BE REPLACED PERIODICALLY.
2011A01660 T00189   19    (34) FIRST GENERATION EQUIPMENT. TRANSFER MACHINES WHERE CLEANING  AND
2011A01660 T00190   20  DRYING  (RECLAIMING)  TAKE  PLACE  IN  SEPARATE MACHINES WITH THE MANUAL
2011A01660 T00191   21  TRANSFER OF ARTICLES FROM ONE MACHINE TO ANOTHER.
2011A01660 T00192   22    (35) FOURTH GENERATION EQUIPMENT. A PRIMARY  CLOSED-LOOP  REFRIGERATED
2011A01660 T00193   23  DRY  CLEANING  MACHINE  THAT  HAS  A  "SECONDARY  CONTROL  SYSTEM" (I.E.
2011A01660 T00194   24  CLOSED-LOOP REFRIGERATED CONDENSER WITH A DRYING SENSOR AND AN  INTEGRAL
2011A01660 T00195   25  CARBON ADSORBER).

2011A01660 T00197   27    (37) FUGITIVE EMISSIONS. THOSE EMISSIONS OF REGULATED AIR CONTAMINANTS
2011A01660 T00198   28  WHICH  COULD NOT REASONABLY PASS THROUGH A STACK, CHIMNEY, VENT OR OTHER

2011A01660 T00199   29  FUNCTIONALLY-EQUIVALENT OPENINGS.

2011A01660 T00204   34  FROM A DRY CLEANING MACHINE WHEN THE VAPORS ARE RECIRCULATING OR VENTING

2011A01660 T00249   20  C1{2}C:CC1{2}. THE CAS REGISTRY NUMBER FOR PERC IS 00127-18-4.
2011A01660 T00250   21    (51-A) PERC-BASED DRY CLEANING FACILITY.  ALL  EQUIPMENT,  DEVICES  OR
2011A01660 T00251   22  APPARATUS  ASSOCIATED  WITH  PERC DRY CLEANING OPERATIONS, INCLUDING BUT
2011A01660 T00252   23  NOT LIMITED TO: DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT; FILTER OR PURIFICATION  SYSTEMS;
2011A01660 T00253   24  WASTE  HOLDING,  TREATMENT OR DISPOSAL SYSTEMS; PERCHLOROETHYLENE SUPPLY
2011A01660 T00254   25  SYSTEMS; DIP TANKS, PUMPS, GASKETS, PIPING, DUCTING, FITTINGS, VALVES OR
2011A01660 T00255   26  FLANGES THAT CONVEY PERC-CONTAMINATED  AIR;  AND  DRY  CLEANING  CONTROL
2011A01660 T00256   27  SYSTEMS.

2011A01660 T00263   34  ALENT CLOSED-LOOP VAPOR RECOVERY SYSTEM APPROVED BY THE DEPARTMENT.
2011A01660 T00264   35    (56) PROCESS VENTILATION EMISSION. AN EMISSION FROM ANY  DRY  CLEANING
2011A01660 T00265   36  MACHINE  NORMALLY  VENTED TO THE OUTER AIR; THAT OCCURS DURING THE AERA-
2011A01660 T00266   37  TION CYCLE AND ALSO WHEN THE MACHINE DOOR IS OPEN; EXCLUDING  DOOR  FANS
2011A01660 T00267   38  ON AZEOTROPIC AND THIRD GENERATION EQUIPMENT.
2011A01660 T00268   39    (57)  REFRIGERATED CONDENSER. A CLOSED-LOOP VAPOR RECOVERY SYSTEM INTO
2011A01660 T00269   40  WHICH PERC VAPORS ARE CONDENSED BY COOLING BELOW THE DEW  POINT  OF  THE
2011A01660 T00270   41  PERC USING A MECHANICAL REFRIGERATED SYSTEM.
2011A01660 T00271   42    (58)  RESIDENTIAL  BUILDING.  ANY  DWELLING  OR HOUSING THAT IS OWNED,
2011A01660 T00272   43  RENTED, OR OCCUPIED BY THE SAME PERSON  FOR  A  PERIOD  OF  ONE  HUNDRED
2011A01660 T00273   44  EIGHTY  DAYS  OR  MORE IN A YEAR, EXCLUDING SHORT-TERM HOUSING SUCH AS A
2011A01660 T00274   45  MOTEL OR HOTEL ROOM RENTED AND OCCUPIED BY THE SAME PERSON FOR A  PERIOD
2011A01660 T00275   46  OF LESS THAN ONE HUNDRED EIGHTY DAYS.
2011A01660 T00276   47    (59)  ROOM ENCLOSURE. A ROOM THAT ENCLOSES THE DRY CLEANING MACHINE OR
2011A01660 T00277   48  EQUIPMENT. IT IS CONSTRUCTED OF MATERIAL THAT IS IMPERMEABLE TO PERC AND
2011A01660 T00278   49  DESIGNED AND OPERATED TO MAINTAIN NEGATIVE PRESSURE AT  ALL  TIMES  THAT
2011A01660 T00279   50  THE  EQUIPMENT  IS  OPERATING  AND IS USED WITH A GENERAL EXHAUST VENTI-
2011A01660 T00280   51  LATION SYSTEM.
2011A01660 T00281   52    (60) SECOND GENERATION EQUIPMENT.  DRY-TO-DRY  VENTED,  UNREFRIGERATED
2011A01660 T00282   53  DRY  CLEANING  MACHINES  PROPERLY  VENTED  TO A CONTROL DEVICE SUCH AS A
2011A01660 T00283   54  CARBON ADSORBER, OR AZEOTROPIC CONTROL DEVICE PLUS A SMALL CARBON ADSOR-
2011A01660 T00284   55  BER, OR EQUIVALENT.

2011A01660 T00290    3  CYCLE BEYOND THE LEVEL ACHIEVABLE WITH A REFRIGERATED  CONDENSER  ALONE.
2011A01660 T00291    4  (E.G. INTEGRAL CARBON ADSORBER USED IN FOURTH GENERATION EQUIPMENT).

2011A01660 T00293    6  AN INTEGRAL PART OF A PRODUCTION PACKAGE WITH A SINGLE MAKE AND MODEL OF

2011A01660 T00301   14  AT  THE  END  OF THE DRYING CYCLE, (E.G. ADSORBERS USED TO CONTROL EMIS-

2011A01660 T00331   44  S 19-1303. VARIANCES.
2011A01660 T00332   45    (1) UNLESS OTHERWISE PRECLUDED BY FEDERAL LAW OR SUBDIVISION 4 OF THIS
2011A01660 T00333   46  SECTION,  THE  DEPARTMENT  MAY, UPON WRITTEN APPLICATION FROM ANY PERSON
2011A01660 T00334   47  WHO IS SUBJECT TO THIS TITLE, GRANT A VARIANCE FROM ONE OR MORE SPECIFIC
2011A01660 T00335   48  PROVISIONS OF THIS TITLE UNDER THE CONDITIONS SET FORTH IN THIS SECTION;
2011A01660 T00336   49  PROVIDED, HOWEVER, THAT VARIANCES SHALL ONLY  BE  GRANTED  UNDER  EXCEP-
2011A01660 T00337   50  TIONAL OR EXTRAORDINARY CIRCUMSTANCES.
2011A01660 T00338   51    (2) EVERY APPLICATION FOR A VARIANCE MUST:
2011A01660 T00339   52    (A)  IDENTIFY THE SPECIFIC PROVISIONS OF THIS TITLE FROM WHICH A VARI-
2011A01660 T00340   53  ANCE IS SOUGHT;
2011A01660 T00341   54    (B) DEMONSTRATE THAT COMPLIANCE WITH THE IDENTIFIED PROVISIONS  WOULD,
2011A01660 T00342   55  ON  THE  BASIS OF CONDITIONS UNIQUE TO THE PERSON'S PARTICULAR SITUATION
2011A01660 T00343   56  IN CONTRAST TO THE REST OF THE INDUSTRY OR ANY SEGMENT THEREOF, TEND  TO
2011A01660 T00344
2011A01660 T00345       A. 1660                             7
2011A01660 T00346
2011A01660 T00347    1  IMPOSE  AN UNREASONABLE ECONOMIC, TECHNOLOGICAL, OR SAFETY BURDEN ON THE
2011A01660 T00348    2  PERSON OR THE PUBLIC; AND
2011A01660 T00349    3    (C)  DEMONSTRATE  THAT  THE PROPOSED ACTIVITY WILL HAVE NO SIGNIFICANT
2011A01660 T00350    4  ADVERSE IMPACT ON THE PUBLIC HEALTH, SAFETY, OR WELFARE, THE ENVIRONMENT
2011A01660 T00351    5  OR NATURAL RESOURCES AND WILL BE CONSISTENT WITH THE PROVISIONS OF  THIS
2011A01660 T00352    6  CHAPTER  AND  THE  PERFORMANCE EXPECTED FROM AN ACTIVITY PERMITTED UNDER
2011A01660 T00353    7  THE PROVISIONS OF THIS TITLE.
2011A01660 T00354    8    (3) IN GRANTING ANY VARIANCE UNDER THIS  SUBDIVISION,  THE  DEPARTMENT
2011A01660 T00355    9  MAY  IMPOSE  SPECIFIC  CONDITIONS  NECESSARY  TO ASSURE THAT THE SUBJECT
2011A01660 T00356   10  ACTIVITY WILL HAVE NO SIGNIFICANT ADVERSE IMPACT ON THE  PUBLIC  HEALTH,
2011A01660 T00357   11  SAFETY, OR WELFARE, THE ENVIRONMENT OR NATURAL RESOURCES.
2011A01660 T00358   12    (4) PHASE-OUT DATES FOR DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT CANNOT BE EXTENDED BY A
2011A01660 T00359   13  VARIANCE.
2011A01660 T00360   14  S 19-1305. PROHIBITIONS.
2011A01660 T00361   15    (1)  THE  USE  OF  ANY  DRY-TO-DRY VENTED OR NON-VENTED EQUIPMENT AS A
2011A01660 T00362   16  TRANSFER MACHINE IS PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00363   17    (2) THE INSTALLATION OF SELF-SERVICE DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT AFTER  THE
2011A01660 T00364   18  EFFECTIVE DATE OF THIS TITLE IS PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00365   19    (3) THE USE OR OFFERING FOR USE OF SELF-SERVICE DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT
2011A01660 T00366   20  SIX MONTHS AFTER THE EFFECTIVE DATE OF THIS TITLE IS PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00367   21    (4)  THE  USE  OF  IMMERSION  HEATERS  TO  EVAPORATE  SOLVENT FROM THE
2011A01660 T00368   22  UNTREATED WATER EFFLUENT OF SOLVENT WATER SEPARATORS IS PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00369   23    (5) EXCEPT AS PROVIDED IN THIS TITLE, PRE-PERMITTING REQUIREMENTS, THE
2011A01660 T00370   24  COMMENCEMENT OF CONSTRUCTION OR MODIFICATION OF A DRY CLEANING  FACILITY
2011A01660 T00371   25  WITHOUT  FIRST  OBTAINING  A  VALID  PERMIT  ISSUED BY THE DEPARTMENT IS
2011A01660 T00372   26  PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00373   27    (6) THE CONSTRUCTION OR OPERATION OF A DRY CLEANING  FACILITY  WITHOUT
2011A01660 T00374   28  FIRST OBTAINING A VALID PERMIT ISSUED BY THE DEPARTMENT IS PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00375   29    (7)  VENTING OF PERC EMISSIONS FROM DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT OR EMISSION
2011A01660 T00376   30  CONTROL DEVICES INTO THE WORKROOM OR FACILITY IS PROHIBITED.
2011A01660 T00377   31    (8) NO NEW PERC-BASED DRY CLEANING FACILITIES SHALL BE PERMITTED WITH-
2011A01660 T00378   32  IN RESIDENTIAL BUILDINGS AFTER THE EFFECTIVE DATE OF THIS SUBDIVISION.
2011A01660 T00379   33  S 19-1307. PRE-PERMITTING REQUIREMENTS FOR EXISTING FACILITIES.
2011A01660 T00380   34    EXISTING FACILITIES MUST COMPLY WITH  THE  FOLLOWING  REQUIREMENTS  IN
2011A01660 T00381   35  ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIMEFRAMES ESTABLISHED IN THIS SECTION IN ADVANCE OF
2011A01660 T00382   36  APPLYING  FOR  AND  OBTAINING PERMITS REQUIRED UNDER THIS SECTION. PRIOR
2011A01660 T00383   37  APPROVALS FROM THE DEPARTMENT ARE NOT NEEDED  FOR  CONSTRUCTION  OF  THE
2011A01660 T00384   38  ROOM  ENCLOSURE,  VAPOR BARRIER, OR CHANGES IN VENT STACK LOCATIONS. NEW
2011A01660 T00385   39  FACILITIES MUST COMPLY WITH ALL THE ITEMS CONTAINED IN THIS SECTION UPON
2011A01660 T00386   40  START-UP.
2011A01660 T00387   41    (1) VAPOR BARRIERS AND GENERAL EXHAUST VENTILATION.
2011A01660 T00388   42    (A) STAND-ALONE DRY CLEANING FACILITIES THAT ARE DESIGNATED  AS  MAJOR
2011A01660 T00389   43  SOURCES,  PURSUANT TO THE NATIONAL PERCHLOROETHYLENE AIR EMISSION STAND-
2011A01660 T00390   44  ARDS FOR DRY CLEANING FACILITIES UNDER 40 CFR 63  SUBPART  M,  AND  THAT
2011A01660 T00391   45  HAVE  TRANSFER  TYPE  MACHINES  SHOULD  HAVE CONTAINED ALL SUCH MACHINES
2011A01660 T00392   46  INSIDE ROOM ENCLOSURES BY SEPTEMBER TWENTY-THIRD,  TWO  THOUSAND  THREE.
2011A01660 T00393   47  EACH ROOM ENCLOSURE MUST BE:
2011A01660 T00394   48    (I) CONSTRUCTED OF MATERIALS IMPERMEABLE TO PERCHLOROETHYLENE; AND,
2011A01660 T00395   49    (II)  DESIGNED  AND  OPERATED  TO MAINTAIN A NEGATIVE PRESSURE AT EACH
2011A01660 T00396   50  OPENING AT ALL TIMES THAT THE MACHINE IS OPERATING.

2011A01660 T00456   51  S 19-1309. EQUIPMENT STANDARDS AND SPECIFICATIONS.
2011A01660 T00457   52    (1) SPECIFIC EQUIPMENT STANDARDS AND EMISSION CONTROL SPECIFICATIONS:
2011A01660 T00458   53    (A) VAPOR BARRIERS. VAPOR BARRIERS MUST, AT A MINIMUM, ENCLOSE THE DRY
2011A01660 T00459   54  CLEANING EQUIPMENT. VAPOR BARRIERS CAN BE CONSTRUCTED OF POLYVINYL CHLO-
2011A01660 T00460   55  RIDE,  PVC  SHEET 22 MIL THICK (0.022 IN.), SHEET METAL, METAL FOIL FACE
2011A01660 T00461   56  COMPOSITE BOARD, OR OTHER EQUIVALENT MATERIALS THAT ARE  IMPERMEABLE  TO
2011A01660 T00462
2011A01660 T00463       A. 1660                             9
2011A01660 T00464
2011A01660 T00465    1  PERC  VAPORS.  VAPOR BARRIERS MUST BE CONSTRUCTED SO THAT ALL JOINTS AND
2011A01660 T00466    2  SEAMS ARE SEALED EXCEPT FOR INLET MAKE-UP AIR AND  EXHAUST  OPENINGS  IN
2011A01660 T00467    3  ENTRY  DOORS, WHICH MUST ONLY BE OPEN WHEN A PERSON IS ENTERING OR EXIT-
2011A01660 T00468    4  ING THE ROOM ENCLOSURE.
2011A01660 T00469    5    (B)  GENERAL  EXHAUST  VENTILATION. DRY CLEANING FACILITIES CO-LOCATED
2011A01660 T00470    6  WITH RESIDENTIAL LIVING QUARTERS, FOOD  SERVICE  ESTABLISHMENTS  OR  ANY
2011A01660 T00471    7  NON-INDUSTRIAL FACILITY MUST BE EQUIPPED WITH A VAPOR BARRIER AND WITH A
2011A01660 T00472    8  GENERAL  EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEM THAT IS COMPLETELY SEPARATE FROM THE
2011A01660 T00473    9  VENTILATION SYSTEM SERVING OTHER AREAS  OF  THE  BUILDING.  THE  GENERAL
2011A01660 T00474   10  EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEM MUST BE LOCATED NEAR THE DRY CLEANING MACHIN-
2011A01660 T00475   11  ERY  OR  CONNECTED  TO  A  SEPARATE  ROOM ENCLOSURE WITH A VAPOR BARRIER
2011A01660 T00476   12  EXHAUSTING EMISSIONS TO THE OUTER AIR. THIS DRY CLEANING GENERAL EXHAUST
2011A01660 T00477   13  VENTILATION SYSTEM MUST BE OPERATED AT ALL TIMES WHEN THE  DRY  CLEANING
2011A01660 T00478   14  MACHINES ARE IN OPERATION, AND DURING MAINTENANCE OPERATIONS AND MUST BE
2011A01660 T00479   15  CAPABLE OF AT LEAST ONE AIR CHANGE PER FIVE MINUTES.
2011A01660 T00480   16    (C) DOOR FAN/LOCAL EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEMS:
2011A01660 T00481   17    (I) ALL FIRST, SECOND AND THIRD GENERATION DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT MUST
2011A01660 T00482   18  BE  EQUIPPED  WITH  A  DOOR  FAN/LOCAL  EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEM. THIS
2011A01660 T00483   19  SYSTEM MUST INCLUDE A MECHANICAL EXHAUST FAN THAT IS ACTIVATED WHEN  THE
2011A01660 T00484   20  LOADING  DOOR  IS  OPEN, DRAWING AIR FROM THE MACHINE DRUM CAUSING FRESH
2011A01660 T00485   21  AIR TO BE DRAWN IN THROUGH THE LOADING DOOR. A MINIMUM INWARD AIR VELOC-
2011A01660 T00486   22  ITY OF 100 FPM, MUST BE MAINTAINED THROUGH THE  EFFECTIVE  DOOR  OPENING
2011A01660 T00487   23  AREA OF THE LOADING DOOR OF THE MACHINE.
2011A01660 T00488   24    (II)  DOOR  FAN/LOCAL EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEMS MUST NOT RECIRCULATE
2011A01660 T00489   25  VAPORS INTO THE WORKROOM AND MUST BE PROPERLY VENTED TO THE OUTER AIR.
2011A01660 T00490   26    (III) DOOR FAN/LOCAL EXHAUST VENTILATION EMISSIONS MUST BE  CONTROLLED
2011A01660 T00491   27  TO  A  DESIGN  EMISSION STANDARD OF FIVE PPM PERC WITH AN IN-USE MAXIMUM
2011A01660 T00492   28  COMPLIANCE STANDARD OF 20 PPM.
2011A01660 T00493   29    (D) PROCESS VENTILATION - INTERIM STANDARDS:
2011A01660 T00494   30    (I) PROCESS VENTS ON FIRST AND SECOND GENERATION MACHINES THAT EXHAUST
2011A01660 T00495   31  DURING THE AERATION CYCLE AND WHEN THE MACHINE  DOOR  IS  OPEN  MUST  BE
2011A01660 T00000.SO DOC A 1660                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01660 T00496   32  VENTED  TO  THE  OUTER AIR ABOVE THE ROOF AND MORE THAN TWENTY-FIVE FEET
2011A01660 T00497   33  FROM ALL OPENINGS IN NEARBY OCCUPANCIES.
2011A01660 T00498   34    (II) PROCESS VENTILATION EMISSIONS  FROM  EXISTING  FIRST  AND  SECOND
2011A01660 T00499   35  GENERATION  VENTED  MACHINES  HAVING  EMISSION  CONTROLS  AS PART OF THE
2011A01660 T00500   36  ORIGINAL EQUIPMENT OR RETROFITTED TO COMPLY WITH THE 100 PPM PERC  EMIS-
2011A01660 T00501   37  SION STANDARD EFFECTIVE MAY TENTH, NINETEEN HUNDRED EIGHTY-ONE UNDER THE
2011A01660 T00502   38  PRIOR  VERSION  OF  THIS TITLE MUST CONTINUE TO MEET THIS STANDARD UNTIL
2011A01660 T00503   39  SUCH TIME AS RETROFITTING, REPLACEMENT, OR SHUTDOWN  IS  REQUIRED  UNDER
2011A01660 T00504   40  THIS SECTION.
2011A01660 T00505   41    (III)  PROCESS  VENTILATION  EMISSIONS FROM EXISTING SECOND GENERATION
2011A01660 T00506   42  MACHINES THAT ARE RETROFITTED WITH  CONTROL  EQUIPMENT  TO  COMPLY  WITH
2011A01660 T00507   43  INTERIM  STANDARDS  ESTABLISHED  UNDER  THIS SECTION MUST BE DESIGNED TO
2011A01660 T00508   44  ACHIEVE A PERC CONCENTRATION OF FIVE PPM OR  LESS  IN  THE  EXHAUST  AND
2011A01660 T00509   45  ACHIEVE  AN  IN-USE  COMPLIANCE STANDARD OF LESS THAN 20 PPM PERC IN THE
2011A01660 T00510   46  EXHAUST.
2011A01660 T00511   47    (IV) THE EXHAUST DAMPER OF A VENTED FIRST OR SECOND GENERATION MACHINE
2011A01660 T00512   48  MUST BE COMPLETELY CLOSED WHEN THE MACHINE IS NOT BEING VENTED, AND MUST
2011A01660 T00513   49  NOT LEAK VAPORS INTO THE WORKROOM OR THE OUTER AIR.
2011A01660 T00514   50    (E) PRIMARY  EMISSION  CONTROL  SYSTEMS.  REFRIGERATED  CONDENSERS  OR
2011A01660 T00515   51  EQUIVALENT  CLOSED  LOOP  VAPOR RECOVERY SYSTEMS MUST MEET THE FOLLOWING
2011A01660 T00516   52  REQUIREMENTS:
2011A01660 T00517   53    (I) REFRIGERATED CONDENSERS MUST BE CAPABLE  OF  ACHIEVING  AN  OUTLET
2011A01660 T00518   54  VAPOR  TEMPERATURE  DOWNSTREAM OF ANY BY-PASS OF THE CONDENSER LESS THAN
2011A01660 T00519   55  OR EQUAL TO 45µF (7.2µC) DURING THE FINAL COOL DOWN CYCLE, AND ACHIEVE A
2011A01660 T00520
2011A01660 T00521       A. 1660                            10
2011A01660 T00522
2011A01660 T00523    1  CONCENTRATION OF 8600 PPM OR LESS PERC IN THE DRUM  UPON  COMPLETION  OF
2011A01660 T00524    2  THE DRYING CYCLE.
2011A01660 T00525    3    (II)  REFRIGERATED CONDENSERS MUST HAVE A GRADUATED THERMOMETER, THER-
2011A01660 T00526    4  MOCOUPLE OR EQUIVALENT INSTRUMENT WITH A MINIMUM RANGE FROM 0µF  (-18µC)
2011A01660 T00527    5  TO  150µF  (66µC),  THAT  MEASURES  THE  TEMPERATURE OF THE OUTLET VAPOR
2011A01660 T00528    6  STREAM DOWNSTREAM OF ANY BY-PASS OF THE CONDENSER, AND IS EASILY VISIBLE
2011A01660 T00529    7  TO THE OPERATOR.
2011A01660 T00530    8    (III) NEW THIRD AND  FOURTH  GENERATION  EQUIPMENT  WITH  REFRIGERATED
2011A01660 T00531    9  CONDENSER   CONTROL   SYSTEMS   MUST   BE   EQUIPPED   WITH   A   DRYING
2011A01660 T00532   10  SENSOR/CONTROLLER THAT EXTENDS THE DRYING TIME  AT  LEAST  FOUR  MINUTES
2011A01660 T00533   11  BEYOND  THE  POINT THAT THE SOLVENT RECOVERY RATE IS LESS THAN 40 ML/MIN
2011A01660 T00534   12  OR SOLVENT VAPOR CONCENTRATION IN THE DRUM IS LESS THAN 8600 PPM PERC.
2011A01660 T00535   13    (IV) THE REFRIGERATED CONDENSER  MUST  BE  OPERATED  WITH  A  DIVERTER
2011A01660 T00536   14  VALVE.
2011A01660 T00537   15     (V)  EQUIVALENT  CLOSED-LOOP  VAPOR RECOVERY SYSTEMS OR OTHER CONTROL
2011A01660 T00538   16  DEVICE MUST USE A TECHNOLOGY THAT HAS BEEN DEMONSTRATED, PURSUANT TO THE
2011A01660 T00539   17  REQUIREMENTS OF THIS TITLE, TO ACHIEVE AT LEAST  90  PERCENT  BY  WEIGHT
2011A01660 T00540   18  EMISSION  REDUCTION  BASED  UPON THE AMOUNT OF PERC ENTERING AND LEAVING
2011A01660 T00541   19  THE CONTROL DEVICE.
2011A01660 T00542   20    (F) A SECONDARY CONTROL SYSTEM MUST:
2011A01660 T00543   21    (I) BE DESIGNED TO FUNCTION WITH A PRIMARY  CONTROL  SYSTEM  COMPLYING
2011A01660 T00544   22  WITH ALL REQUIREMENTS FOR THIRD GENERATION EQUIPMENT.
2011A01660 T00545   23    (II)  BE  CAPABLE  OF REDUCING THE PERC CONCENTRATION IN THE DRUM FROM
2011A01660 T00546   24  8600 PPM OR GREATER TO 300 PPM.
2011A01660 T00547   25    (III) ANY INTEGRAL CARBON ADSORBER USED AS A SECONDARY CONTROL  SYSTEM
2011A01660 T00548   26  MUST  BE  SIZED CORRECTLY FOR THE MACHINE AND BE CAPABLE OF REDUCING THE
2011A01660 T00549   27  PERC CONCENTRATION IN THE DRUM FROM 8,600 PPM OR GREATER TO 300  PPM  OR
2011A01660 T00550   28  LESS.
2011A01660 T00551   29    (IV)  THE  INTEGRAL  CARBON  ADSORBER MUST BE DESIGNED FOR NON-CONTACT
2011A01660 T00552   30  STEAM OR HOT AIR STRIPPING OPERATION, AND MUST BE STRIPPED  OR  DESORBED
2011A01660 T00553   31  IN  ACCORDANCE  WITH  MANUFACTURER'S  INSTRUCTIONS  OR  AT LEAST WEEKLY,
2011A01660 T00554   32  WHICHEVER IS MORE STRINGENT.
2011A01660 T00555   33    (G) SPILL CONTAINMENT. ALL NEW THIRD AND FOURTH GENERATION,  OR  USED,
2011A01660 T00556   34  REINSTALLED  DRY  CLEANING  EQUIPMENT  MUST  BE  EQUIPPED  WITH  A SPILL
2011A01660 T00557   35  CONTAINMENT SYSTEM CAPABLE OF CONTAINING 125 PERCENT OF THE CAPACITY  OF
2011A01660 T00558   36  THE  LARGEST  DRY  CLEANING  PERC TANK OR VESSEL ASSOCIATED WITH THE DRY
2011A01660 T00559   37  CLEANING MACHINE.
2011A01660 T00560   38    (2) TO DETERMINE WHICH STANDARDS WILL APPLY TO A PARTICULAR DRY CLEAN-
2011A01660 T00561   39  ING FACILITY, FIRST DETERMINE WHETHER THE FACILITY IS  NEW  OR  EXISTING
2011A01660 T00562   40  (ONE  THAT  EXISTED  PRIOR  TO  THE  EFFECTIVE DATE OF THIS TITLE). THEN
2011A01660 T00563   41  DETERMINE WHETHER THE FACILITY IS A  STAND-ALONE  OR  IS  LOCATED  IN  A
2011A01660 T00564   42  MIXED-USE  BUILDING. IF IN A MIXED-USE BUILDING, DETERMINE WHETHER IT IS
2011A01660 T00565   43  A COMMERCIAL OR RESIDENTIAL BUILDING. FINALLY, FOR EACH PIECE OF  EQUIP-
2011A01660 T00566   44  MENT THERE ARE TWO PRIMARY ISSUES ADDRESSED IN THE REGULATIONS--THE TYPE
2011A01660 T00567   45  OF  EMISSIONS  CONTROL  AND THE LOCATION OF ANY PROCESS VENTS (SEE DEFI-
2011A01660 T00568   46  NITION OF PROCESS VENT).  PROCESS  VENTS  APPLY  ONLY  TO  TRANSFER  AND
2011A01660 T00569   47  DRY-TO-DRY  VENTED  EQUIPMENT, NOT TO DOOR FANS, GENERAL OR OTHER VENTI-
2011A01660 T00570   48  LATION.
2011A01660 T00571   49    IN ALL, THERE ARE SIX DIFFERENT CATEGORIES FOR WHICH EQUIPMENT  STAND-
2011A01660 T00572   50  ARDS ARE PROVIDED AS FOLLOWS:

2011A01660 T00737   38    (A)  IF THE PROCESS VENT IS LOCATED ABOVE THE ROOF AND MORE THAN TWEN-
2011A01660 T00738   39  TY-FIVE FEET FROM ALL OPENINGS IN NEARBY OCCUPANCIES, AND IF THE  EQUIP-
2011A01660 T00739   40  MENT  HAS  BEEN  PREVIOUSLY RETROFITTED TO COMPLY WITH THE LESS THAN 100
2011A01660 T00740   41  PPM PERC VENTED EMISSION LEVEL AND IS OPERATING IN COMPLIANCE WITH  THAT
2011A01660 T00741   42  EMISSION  LEVEL, THE EQUIPMENT MUST BE REMOVED FROM SERVICE BY SEPTEMBER
2011A01660 T00742   43  TWENTY-SECOND, TWO THOUSAND TWELVE.
2011A01660 T00743   44    (B) IF  THE  PROCESS  VENT  IS  NOT  ABOVE  THE  ROOF  AND  MORE  THAN
2011A01660 T00744   45  TWENTY-FIVE  FEET  FROM  ALL  OPENINGS  IN NEARBY OCCUPANCIES, OR IF THE
2011A01660 T00745   46  EQUIPMENT HAS NOT PREVIOUSLY BEEN RETROFITTED OR IS  NOT  IN  COMPLIANCE
2011A01660 T00746   47  WITH  THE  LESS  THAN 100 PPM PERC EMISSION LEVEL, THE EQUIPMENT MUST BE
2011A01660 T00747   48  REMOVED FROM SERVICE WITHIN SIX MONTHS AFTER THE EFFECTIVE DATE OF  THIS
2011A01660 T00748   49  TITLE.
2011A01660 T00749   50    (C)  A  VAPOR  BARRIER AND GENERAL VENTILATION ARE REQUIRED WITHIN SIX
2011A01660 T00750   51  MONTHS AFTER THE EFFECTIVE DATE OF  THIS  TITLE  AS  SPECIFIED  IN  THIS
2011A01660 T00751   52  SECTION.

2011A01660 T00858   42  S 19-1311. LEAK INSPECTION AND SELF MONITORING REQUIREMENTS.
2011A01660 T00859   43    (1) LEAK CHECK REQUIREMENTS. THE TRAINED OPERATOR MUST INSPECT THE DRY
2011A01660 T00860   44  CLEANING SYSTEM FOR PERCEPTIBLE (LIQUID AND VAPOR) LEAKS AND OTHER FUGI-
2011A01660 T00861   45  TIVE EMISSIONS. THE TRAINED OPERATOR OR  A  DESIGNEE,  MUST  RECORD  THE
2011A01660 T00862   46  STATUS  OF  EACH  COMPONENT  ON  A CHECKLIST SUPPLIED BY THE DEPARTMENT.
2011A01660 T00863   47  COMPLETED CHECKLISTS MUST BE KEPT FOR AT LEAST FIVE YEARS FROM THE  DATE
2011A01660 T00864   48  OF THE INSPECTION.
2011A01660 T00865   49    (A)  THE  DRY  CLEANING  SYSTEM MUST BE THOROUGHLY INSPECTED, AT LEAST
2011A01660 T00866   50  WEEKLY, FOR VAPOR LEAKS USING ONE OF THE FOLLOWING FOR  DETECTING  VAPOR
2011A01660 T00867   51  LEAKS:
2011A01660 T00868   52    (I) A HALOGENATED-HYDROCARBON DETECTOR;
2011A01660 T00869   53    (II) A PORTABLE GAS ANALYZER;
2011A01660 T00870   54    (III) AN AIR SAMPLING PUMP AND COLORIMETRIC TUBE; OR
2011A01660 T00871   55    (IV) AN ALTERNATIVE METHOD APPROVED BY THE DEPARTMENT.

2011A01660 T00913   39    (7) ANY LIQUID LEAK, VAPOR LEAK, OR MALFUNCTION THAT HAS BEEN DETECTED
2011A01660 T00914   40  BY THE OPERATOR MUST BE NOTED ON THE CHECKLIST AND, IF AT ALL  POSSIBLE,
2011A01660 T00915   41  REPAIRED  IMMEDIATELY.  IF  THE  LEAK  CANNOT BE REPAIRED AT THE TIME OF
2011A01660 T00916   42  DETECTION, THE LEAKING COMPONENT MUST BE PHYSICALLY MARKED OR TAGGED  IN
2011A01660 T00917   43  A MANNER THAT IS READILY OBSERVABLE BY AN INSPECTOR AND MUST BE REPAIRED
2011A01660 T00918   44  WITHIN  TWENTY-FOUR HOURS OF DETECTION, UNLESS REPAIR PARTS ARE UNAVAIL-
2011A01660 T00919   45  ABLE.
2011A01660 T00920   46    (A) IF REPAIR PARTS ARE NOT AVAILABLE AT THE FACILITY, THE PARTS  MUST
2011A01660 T00921   47  BE ORDERED WITHIN TWO WORKING DAYS OF DETECTING SUCH A LEAK. SUCH REPAIR
2011A01660 T00922   48  PARTS  MUST BE INSTALLED WITHIN FIVE WORKING DAYS AFTER RECEIPT.  EQUIP-
2011A01660 T00923   49  MENT WITH A LEAK THAT HAS NOT BEEN REPAIRED BY THE END OF THE  FIFTEENTH
2011A01660 T00924   50  WORKING  DAY  AFTER  DETECTION  MUST  NOT  BE OPERATED UNTIL THE LEAK IS
2011A01660 T00925   51  REPAIRED, UNLESS THE FACILITY OWNER OR OPERATOR RECEIVES  A  LEAK-REPAIR
2011A01660 T00926   52  EXTENSION FROM THE DEPARTMENT.
2011A01660 T00927   53    (B)  THE  DEPARTMENT  MAY  GRANT A LEAK-REPAIR EXTENSION TO A FACILITY
2011A01660 T00928   54  OWNER FOR A SINGLE PERIOD OF THIRTY DAYS  OR  LESS,  IF  THE  DEPARTMENT
2011A01660 T00929   55  MAKES THESE FINDINGS:
2011A01660 T00930
2011A01660 T00931       A. 1660                            17
2011A01660 T00932
2011A01660 T00933    1    (I)  THE  DELAY  IN  REPAIRING THE LEAK COULD NOT HAVE BEEN AVOIDED BY
2011A01660 T00934    2  ACTION ON THE PART OF THE FACILITY OWNER OR OPERATOR;
2011A01660 T00935    3    (II)  THE FACILITY OWNER AND OPERATOR USED REASONABLE PREVENTIVE MEAS-
2011A01660 T00936    4  URES AND ACTED PROMPTLY TO INITIATE THE REPAIR;
2011A01660 T00937    5    (III) THE LEAK WILL NOT SIGNIFICANTLY INCREASE PERC EXPOSURE NEAR  THE
2011A01660 T00938    6  FACILITY; AND
2011A01660 T00939    7    (IV) THE FACILITY IS IN COMPLIANCE WITH ALL OTHER REQUIREMENTS OF THIS
2011A01660 T00940    8  SECTION AND HAS A HISTORY OF COMPLIANCE.
2011A01660 T00941    9    (C) SUCH EXTENSION MAY BE GRANTED VERBALLY, BUT MUST BE FOLLOWED UP BY
2011A01660 T00942   10  A WRITTEN CONFIRMATION WITHIN THREE DAYS.

2011A01660 T00944   12  ON THE CHECKLIST.

2011A01660 T00951   19  ANY PART  OF  THE  DRY  CLEANING  SYSTEM  IS  A  VIOLATION;  EXCEPT  FOR

2011A01660 T00953   21  SYSTEM COMPONENTS FOR INSPECTION OR REPAIR.

2011A01660 T00955   23  THAT  HAS  BEEN  DETECTED BY THE OPERATOR MUST BE NOTED ON THE CHECKLIST

2011A01660 T00957   25  S 19-1313. OPERATION AND MAINTENANCE REQUIREMENTS.
2011A01660 T00958   26    (1) DRY CLEANING FACILITIES MUST BE MAINTAINED AND OPERATED  TO  MINI-
2011A01660 T00959   27  MIZE THE RELEASE OF PERC TO THE ENVIRONMENT.
2011A01660 T00960   28    (2)  THE  OPERATOR MUST OPERATE AND MAINTAIN ALL COMPONENTS OF THE DRY
2011A01660 T00961   29  CLEANING SYSTEM IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE REQUIREMENTS OF  THIS  TITLE  AND
2011A01660 T00962   30  THE  CONDITIONS  SPECIFIED  IN  A FACILITY'S OPERATING PERMIT. FOR OPER-
2011A01660 T00963   31  ATIONS NOT SPECIFICALLY ADDRESSED, THE COMPONENTS MUST BE  OPERATED  AND
2011A01660 T00964   32  MAINTAINED  IN  ACCORDANCE  WITH THE MANUFACTURER'S RECOMMENDATIONS. THE
2011A01660 T00965   33  FACILITY OPERATOR MUST RETAIN, ON-SITE, A COPY OF THE DESIGN  SPECIFICA-
2011A01660 T00966   34  TIONS  AND  THE  OPERATING MANUALS FOR EACH DRY CLEANING SYSTEM AND EACH
2011A01660 T00967   35  EMISSION CONTROL DEVICE LOCATED AT THE DRY CLEANING FACILITY.
2011A01660 T00968   36    (3) THE DEPARTMENT SHALL PROVIDE AN OPERATION AND  MAINTENANCE  CHECK-
2011A01660 T00969   37  LIST  TO  THE  FACILITY. EACH OPERATION AND MAINTENANCE FUNCTION AND THE
2011A01660 T00970   38  DATE PERFORMED MUST BE RECORDED ON THE CHECKLIST.  COMPLETED  CHECKLISTS
2011A01660 T00971   39  MUST  BE MAINTAINED ON SITE FOR AT LEAST FIVE YEARS FROM THE DATE OF THE
2011A01660 T00972   40  CHECKLIST.
2011A01660 T00973   41    (4) OPERATORS MUST COMPLY WITH THE FOLLOWING OPERATION AND MAINTENANCE
2011A01660 T00974   42  REQUIREMENTS, AS APPLICABLE:
2011A01660 T00975   43    (A) FOURTH GENERATION MACHINES.
2011A01660 T00976   44    (I) REFRIGERATED  CONDENSERS  MUST  BE  OPERATED  IN  ACCORDANCE  WITH
2011A01660 T00977   45  MANUFACTURER'S SPECIFICATIONS.
2011A01660 T00978   46    (II)  INTEGRAL REFRIGERATED CONDENSERS MUST BE OPERATED TO ENSURE THAT
2011A01660 T00979   47  EXHAUST GASES ARE RECIRCULATED UNTIL THE AIR-VAPOR STREAM TEMPERATURE IS
2011A01660 T00980   48  45µF OR LESS AT THE OUTLET. THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN  THE  TEMPERATURE  OF
2011A01660 T00981   49  THE AIR-PERC GAS VAPOR STREAM EXITING THE REFRIGERATED CONDENSER MUST BE
2011A01660 T00982   50  GREATER  THAN  OR  EQUAL TO 20µ F (11.1µC). THE TEMPERATURE DIFFERENTIAL
2011A01660 T00983   51  MUST BE DETERMINED AT LEAST WEEKLY WITH A THERMOMETER WITH A TEMPERATURE
2011A01660 T00984   52  RANGE  OF  FROM  32µF  (0µC)  TO  120µF  (48.9µC)  TO  AN  ACCURACY   OF
2011A01660 T00985   53  ñ2µF(1.1µC).
2011A01660 T00986   54    (III)  VAPOR ADSORBERS USED WITH A PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEM OR SECONDARY
2011A01660 T00987   55  CONTROL SYSTEM MUST BE OPERATED TO ENSURE THAT EXHAUST GASES ARE  RECIR-
2011A01660 T00988   56  CULATED AT THE TEMPERATURE SPECIFIED FOR OPTIMUM ADSORPTION.

2011A01660 T00992    1    (IV)  CARTRIDGE  FILTERS  AND  ADSORPTIVE  CARTRIDGE  FILTERS  MUST BE
2011A01660 T00993    2  HANDLED USING ONE OF THE FOLLOWING METHODS:
2011A01660 T00994    3    (A)  DRAINED  IN THE FILTER HOUSING, BEFORE DISPOSAL, FOR NO LESS THAN
2011A01660 T00995    4  TWENTY-FOUR HOURS FOR CARTRIDGE FILTER AND FORTY-EIGHT HOURS FOR ADSORP-
2011A01660 T00996    5  TIVE CARTRIDGE FILTERS.
2011A01660 T00997    6    IF THE FILTERS ARE THEN TRANSFERRED TO A SEPARATE  DEVICE  TO  FURTHER
2011A01660 T00998    7  REDUCE  THE VOLUME OF PERC, THIS TREATMENT MUST BE DONE IN A SYSTEM THAT
2011A01660 T00999    8  ROUTES ANY VAPOR TO A  PRIMARY  CLOSED  LOOP  CONTROL  SYSTEM,  WITH  NO
2011A01660 T01000    9  EXHAUST  TO  THE ATMOSPHERE. SUCH TRANSFER MUST BE PERFORMED CLOSING THE
2011A01660 T01001   10  FILTER HOUSING AS SOON AS POSSIBLE TO MINIMIZE VAPOR LEAKS. THE  GENERAL
2011A01660 T01002   11  EXHAUST VENTILATION SYSTEM MUST BE OPERATED DURING THIS ACTIVITY.
2011A01660 T01003   12    (B)  DRIED, STRIPPED, SPARGED, OR OTHERWISE TREATED, WITHIN THE SEALED
2011A01660 T01004   13  FILTER HOUSING, TO REDUCE THE VOLUME OF PERC CONTAINED IN THE FILTER.
2011A01660 T01005   14    (V) ALL STEAM AND CONDENSING COILS MUST BE MAINTAINED TO  BE  FREE  OF
2011A01660 T01006   15  LINT AND HARD LINT BUILD-UP ON INTERIOR SURFACES.
2011A01660 T01007   16    (VI)  FOR  DRY  CLEANING  EQUIPMENT  EQUIPPED WITH A DOOR FAN, SUCH AS
2011A01660 T01008   17  WHERE THE APPLICABLE DRUM CONCENTRATION UPON MACHINE OPENING  CANNOT  BE
2011A01660 T01009   18  MET,  THE  OPERATOR MUST USE A PORTABLE VELOMETER OR EQUIVALENT MEASURE-
2011A01660 T01010   19  MENT INSTRUMENT TO VERIFY THAT THE REQUIRED 100 FPM INWARD AIR  VELOCITY
2011A01660 T01011   20  IS  MAINTAINED  THROUGH THE EFFECTIVE DOOR OPENING WHEN THE LOADING DOOR
2011A01660 T01012   21  IS OPEN. THE INWARD AIR VELOCITY MUST BE CHECKED ON A WEEKLY BASIS.

2011A01660 T01051    1    (C) SECOND GENERATION MACHINES.
2011A01660 T01052    2    (I)  A  VENTED  MACHINE  OPERATED  WITH  FULL-SIZED  CARBON  ADSORBERS
2011A01660 T01053    3  (DRY-TO-DRY VENTED) THAT FUNCTION DURING THE DRYING CYCLE MUST MEET  THE
2011A01660 T01054    4  FOLLOWING REQUIREMENTS:
2011A01660 T01055    5    (A)  DESORPTION  MUST  BE  PERFORMED AT THE FREQUENCY SPECIFIED BY THE
2011A01660 T01056    6  MANUFACTURER OR AS SPECIFIED BY THIS TITLE, WHICHEVER IS MORE STRINGENT.
2011A01660 T01057    7  THE MINIMUM FREQUENCY FOR DESORPTION OF FULL-SIZE  CARBON  UNITS  IS  AS
2011A01660 T01058    8  FOLLOWS,  EACH  TIME  ALL DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT EXHAUSTED TO THE DEVICE
2011A01660 T01059    9  HAS CLEANED A TOTAL OF THREE POUNDS OF ARTICLES FOR EACH POUND OF  ACTI-
2011A01660 T01060   10  VATED  CARBON. DESORPTION MUST BE PERFORMED WITH THE MINIMUM STEAM PRES-
2011A01660 T01061   11  SURE AND AIR FLOW CAPACITY SPECIFIED BY THE MANUFACTURER.
2011A01660 T01062   12    (B) ONCE DESORPTION IS COMPLETE, THE CARBON BED MUST  BE  FULLY  DRIED
2011A01660 T01063   13  ACCORDING TO THE MANUFACTURER'S INSTRUCTIONS.
2011A01660 T01064   14    (C)  NO  PERC  VAPORS  MAY  BYPASS  THE CARBON ADSORBER TO THE OUTDOOR
2011A01660 T01065   15  ATMOSPHERE AT ANY TIME, NOR BE RECIRCULATED INTO THE FACILITY.
2011A01660 T01066   16    (D) THE FILTER LOCATED IN FRONT OF THE CARBON ADSORBER MUST BE CHECKED
2011A01660 T01067   17  AND CLEANED WEEKLY.
2011A01660 T01068   18    (E) FOR DRY CLEANING  EQUIPMENT  IN  MIXED-USE  SETTINGS,  THE  CARBON
2011A01660 T01069   19  ADSORBER  VENT  MUST BE TESTED WEEKLY USING COLORIMETRIC DETECTOR TUBES.
2011A01660 T01070   20  TEST RESULTS MUST BE RECORDED ON THE CHECKLIST. TEST RESULTS OF FIVE PPM
2011A01660 T01071   21  OR GREATER PERC REQUIRE AN IMMEDIATE STRIPPING OF THE CARBON ADSORBER.
2011A01660 T01072   22    (II) SMALL EXTERNAL  CARBON  ADSORBERS  USED  FOR  AZEOTROPIC  CONTROL
2011A01660 T01073   23  SYSTEMS, MUST BE STRIPPED AT LEAST WEEKLY WHEN IN USE. IF NOT IN CONTIN-
2011A01660 T01074   24  UOUS DAILY USE, ADSORBERS MUST BE STRIPPED AFTER THEY HAVE BEEN USED FOR
2011A01660 T01075   25  TEN DAYS.
2011A01660 T01076   26    (A)  SMALL  EXTERNAL  CARBON  ADSORBERS  MUST BE VENTED TO OUTSIDE THE
2011A01660 T01077   27  BUILDING AND MUST NOT RECIRCULATE VAPOR INTO THE FACILITY.
2011A01660 T01078   28    (B) SMALL EXTERNAL CARBON ADSORBERS USED IN MIXED-USE SETTINGS MUST BE
2011A01660 T01079   29  TESTED WEEKLY USING COLORIMETRIC DETECTOR TUBES OR EQUIVALENT  MEASURING
2011A01660 T01080   30  DEVICES.  TEST  RESULTS  MUST BE RECORDED ON THE INSPECTION CHECKLIST. A
2011A01660 T01081   31  TEST RESULT OF FIVE PPM PERC OR GREATER REQUIRE AN  IMMEDIATE  STRIPPING
2011A01660 T01082   32  OF THE CARBON ADSORBER.
2011A01660 T01083   33    (III) THE EXHAUST DAMPER OF A VENTED MACHINE MUST BE COMPLETELY CLOSED
2011A01660 T01084   34  WHEN  THE  MACHINE  IS NOT BEING VENTED AND MUST BE REPAIRED OR REPLACED
2011A01660 T01085   35  WITHIN FIVE WORKING DAYS IF MALFUNCTIONING.

2011A01660 T01164   55  S 19-1315. PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER MANAGEMENT.
2011A01660 T01165
2011A01660 T01166       A. 1660                            21
2011A01660 T01167
2011A01660 T01168    1    PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER GENERATED BY FACILITIES SUBJECT  TO  THIS
2011A01660 T01169    2  TITLE MUST BE MANAGED AS FOLLOWS:
2011A01660 T01170    3    (1) PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER DISCHARGES.
2011A01660 T01171    4    (A)  PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER THAT IS DISCHARGED TO A SEWER SYSTEM
2011A01660 T01172    5  MUST BE TREATED BY PHYSICAL  SEPARATION  (WATER  SEPARATOR)  AND  DOUBLE
2011A01660 T01173    6  CARBON  FILTRATION,  OR AN EQUIVALENT CONTROL WHICH HAS BEEN APPROVED BY
2011A01660 T01174    7  THE DEPARTMENT, WHICH HAS BEEN PROPERLY DESIGNED TO ASSURE  AN  EFFLUENT
2011A01660 T01175    8  QUALITY THAT:
2011A01660 T01176    9    (I)  IS  LESS  THAN  OR EQUAL TO 20 PPB PERC WITHOUT PERC EVAPORATION;
2011A01660 T01177   10  AND,
2011A01660 T01178   11    (II) CONFORMS TO APPROPRIATE LOCAL SEWER USE ORDINANCES.
2011A01660 T01179   12    (B) ALL PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER DISCHARGES TO SURFACE AND GROUND-
2011A01660 T01180   13  WATERS MUST CONFORM TO THE REQUIREMENTS OF THIS CHAPTER.
2011A01660 T01181   14    (2) EVAPORATION OF PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER.
2011A01660 T01182   15    PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER THAT IS EVAPORATED  MUST  BE  TREATED  BY
2011A01660 T01183   16  PHYSICAL SEPARATION (WATER SEPARATOR) AND DOUBLE CARBON FILTRATION PRIOR
2011A01660 T01184   17  TO EVAPORATION.
2011A01660 T01185   18  S 19-1317. HAZARDOUS WASTE MANAGEMENT.
2011A01660 T01186   19    (1)  ANY PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTES GENERATED MUST BE MANAGED IN ACCORD-
2011A01660 T01187   20  ANCE WITH THIS CHAPTER.  PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER MUST BE HANDLED AS
2011A01660 T01188   21  PROVIDED IN SECTION 19-1315 OF THIS TITLE.
2011A01660 T00000.SO DOC A 1660                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01660 T01189   22    (2) ALL PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTES (INCLUDING SPENT  CARTRIDGE  FILTERS,
2011A01660 T01190   23  SPENT  CARBON, STILL BOTTOMS, AND LINT) MUST BE STORED IN TIGHTLY SEALED
2011A01660 T01191   24  CONTAINERS, WHICH ARE IMPERMEABLE TO THE SOLVENT; SO  THAT  NO  PERC  IS
2011A01660 T01192   25  EMITTED TO THE ATMOSPHERE.
2011A01660 T01193   26    (3)  CONTAINERS  MUST  BE APPROPRIATELY LABELED AND STORED IN A DESIG-
2011A01660 T01194   27  NATED AREA.
2011A01660 T01195   28    (4) CONTAINERS MUST BE IN GOOD  CONDITION  AND  MUST  BE  KEPT  CLOSED
2011A01660 T01196   29  EXCEPT WHEN NECESSARY TO ADD OR REMOVE WASTE.
2011A01660 T01197   30    (5) RECEIPTS OR RECORDS SHOWING THE DATE AND VOLUME OF HAZARDOUS WASTE
2011A01660 T01198   31  SHIPMENTS MUST BE RETAINED FOR FIVE YEARS.
2011A01660 T01199   32  S 19-1319. EMERGENCY RESPONSE.
2011A01660 T01200   33    (1)  DRY  CLEANING  SYSTEMS  MUST BE OPERATED AND MAINTAINED TO ENSURE
2011A01660 T01201   34  THAT PERC RELEASES ARE CONTAINED AND DO NOT MIGRATE TO SEWER SYSTEMS  OR
2011A01660 T01202   35  GROUNDWATER.
2011A01660 T01203   36    (A) FOR EXISTING DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT:
2011A01660 T01204   37    (I) FLOOR DRAINS AND FLOORING IN THE VICINITY OF THE EQUIPMENT MUST BE
2011A01660 T01205   38  SEALED SO AS TO BE IMPERMEABLE TO SPILLS, OR
2011A01660 T01206   39    (II)  TEMPORARY DIKES, BERMS AND CONTAINMENT DEVICES MUST BE PLACED IN
2011A01660 T01207   40  AREAS WHERE SPILLS ARE MOST LIKELY TO OCCUR AND PROCEDURES FOR  PREVENT-
2011A01660 T01208   41  ING SPILL MIGRATION MUST BE ESTABLISHED AND FOLLOWED.
2011A01660 T01209   42    (B) FOR NEW DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT, A SPILL CONTAINMENT SYSTEM MUST BE
2011A01660 T01210   43  INSTALLED UNDER THE EQUIPMENT.
2011A01660 T01211   44    (2)  IN THE EVENT OF A PERC RELEASE, THE OWNER, OPERATOR OR A DESIGNEE
2011A01660 T01212   45  MUST TAKE ALL REASONABLE MEASURES TO ENSURE THE  RELEASE  IS  CONTAINED.
2011A01660 T01213   46  THESE  MEASURES  MUST  INCLUDE, WHERE APPLICABLE, STOPPING PROCESSES AND
2011A01660 T01214   47  OPERATIONS, INCREASING ROOM EXHAUST VENTILATION, COLLECTING AND CONTAIN-
2011A01660 T01215   48  ING RELEASED PERC AND REMOVING AND MAINTAINING CONTAINERS.
2011A01660 T01216   49    (3) IF THE FACILITY OPERATOR DETERMINES THE FACILITY HAS HAD AN UNCON-
2011A01660 T01217   50  TAINABLE RELEASE, FIRE OR EXPLOSION, HE OR SHE MUST REPORT THE  FINDINGS
2011A01660 T01218   51  TO THE DEPARTMENT AND APPROPRIATE EMERGENCY RESPONSE AGENCIES IMMEDIATE-
2011A01660 T01219   52  LY.
2011A01660 T01220   53    (4)  ANY  EMERGENCY RESPONSE ACTION MUST BE RECORDED. THIS RECORD MUST
2011A01660 T01221   54  INCLUDE, AT A MINIMUM:

2011A01660 T01223   56  DENT OF THE DRY CLEANING SYSTEM;

2011A01660 T01229    3  S 19-1321. REPORTING AND RECORDKEEPING.
2011A01660 T01230    4    (1)  OPERATORS  OF ALL DRY CLEANING FACILITIES OR THEIR DESIGNEES MUST
2011A01660 T01231    5  RECORD THE FOLLOWING:
2011A01660 T01232    6    (A) THE DATE, DURATION AND NATURE OF ANY MALFUNCTION, SPILL, INCIDENT,
2011A01660 T01233    7  OR EMERGENCY RESPONSE AT THE FACILITY;
2011A01660 T01234    8    (B) THE DATE OF MAINTENANCE ON ANY AIR CLEANING COMPONENT  OR  EXHAUST
2011A01660 T01235    9  SYSTEM  (SUCH  AS THE REGENERATION AND/OR REPLACEMENT OF THE CARBON IN A
2011A01660 T01236   10  CARBON ADSORBER);
2011A01660 T01237   11    (C) THE NUMBER OF LOADS BETWEEN REGENERATIONS; CLEANING  AND  REPLACE-
2011A01660 T01238   12  MENT  OF  LINT  FILTERS,  AND  CARBON  ADSORBER  PRE-FILTERS;  REPAIR OR
2011A01660 T01239   13  REPLACEMENT OF EXHAUST FANS;
2011A01660 T01240   14    (D) THE AMOUNT OF ACTIVATED CARBON IN CARBON ADSORBERS (DRY WEIGHT  IN
2011A01660 T01241   15  POUNDS);
2011A01660 T01242   16    (E) THE DATE OF MAINTENANCE OF DRYING SENSORS;
2011A01660 T01243   17    (F) THE DATE AND VOLUME OF HAZARDOUS WASTE SHIPMENTS; AND
2011A01660 T01244   18    (G)  THE  DATES  OF PERC-CONTAMINATED WASTEWATER TREATMENT UNIT CARBON
2011A01660 T01245   19  CARTRIDGE REPLACEMENT.
2011A01660 T01246   20    (2) EACH OWNER OR OPERATOR  OF  A  DRY  CLEANING  FACILITY  MUST  KEEP
2011A01660 T01247   21  RECEIPTS OF PERC PURCHASES, A LOG OF THE FOLLOWING INFORMATION, MAINTAIN
2011A01660 T01248   22  SUCH  INFORMATION  ON  SITE  AND PROVIDE IT UPON REQUEST FOR A PERIOD OF
2011A01660 T01249   23  FIVE YEARS:
2011A01660 T01250   24    (A) THE VOLUME OF PERC PURCHASED EACH MONTH BY THE DRY CLEANING FACIL-
2011A01660 T01251   25  ITY AS RECORDED FROM PERC PURCHASES; IF NO PERC IS  PURCHASED  DURING  A
2011A01660 T01252   26  GIVEN MONTH THEN THE OWNER OR OPERATOR WOULD ENTER ZERO GALLONS INTO THE
2011A01660 T01253   27  LOG;
2011A01660 T01254   28    (B)  THE  OWNER  OR OPERATOR MUST PERFORM THE FOLLOWING CALCULATION ON
2011A01660 T01255   29  THE FIRST DAY OF EVERY MONTH:
2011A01660 T01256   30    (I) SUM THE VOLUME OF ALL PERC PURCHASES MADE IN EACH OF THE  PREVIOUS
2011A01660 T01257   31  TWELVE MONTHS, AS RECORDED IN THE LOG.
2011A01660 T01258   32    (II)  IF  NO  PERC PURCHASES WERE MADE IN A GIVEN MONTH, THEN THE PERC
2011A01660 T01259   33  CONSUMPTION FOR THAT MONTH IS ZERO GALLONS.
2011A01660 T01260   34    (III) THE TOTAL SUM CALCULATED IS THE YEARLY PERC CONSUMPTION  AT  THE
2011A01660 T01261   35  FACILITY.
2011A01660 T01262   36    (3)  EACH OWNER OR OPERATOR OF A DRY CLEANING FACILITY MUST RECORD THE
2011A01660 T01263   37  FOLLOWING INFORMATION ON AN INSPECTION CHECKLIST.
2011A01660 T01264   38    (A) THE DATES WHEN THE DRY CLEANING SYSTEM  COMPONENTS  ARE  INSPECTED
2011A01660 T01265   39  FOR  PERCEPTIBLE  LEAKS  AS  SPECIFIED  UNDER THE INSPECTION AND TESTING
2011A01660 T01266   40  REQUIREMENTS, AND THE NAME OR LOCATION OF DRY CLEANING SYSTEM COMPONENTS
2011A01660 T01267   41  WHERE PERCEPTIBLE LEAKS ARE DETECTED;
2011A01660 T01268   42    (B) THE DATE, TIME AND COLORIMETRIC DETECTOR TUBE MONITORING  RESULTS,
2011A01660 T01269   43  IF A CARBON ADSORBER IS USED FOR PRIMARY OR SECONDARY EMISSION CONTROL;
2011A01660 T01270   44    (C)  THE  DATE,  TIME  AND  TEMPERATURE  SENSOR MONITORING RESULTS FOR
2011A01660 T01271   45  REFRIGERATED CONDENSERS;
2011A01660 T01272   46    (D) THE DATES OF REPAIR AND RECORDS OF WRITTEN OR  VERBAL  ORDERS  FOR
2011A01660 T01273   47  REPAIR  PARTS  TO DEMONSTRATE COMPLIANCE WITH THE INSPECTION AND TESTING
2011A01660 T01274   48  REQUIREMENTS, IN SECTION 19-1311 OF THIS TITLE.
2011A01660 T01275   49    (4) EACH OWNER OR OPERATOR OF A DRY CLEANING FACILITY MUST  RETAIN  ON
2011A01660 T01276   50  SITE  COPIES  OF THE OPERATION AND MAINTENANCE CHECKLISTS AND COMPLIANCE
2011A01660 T01277   51  INSPECTION REPORTING FORMS.

2011A01660 T01281   55  DRY CLEANING FACILITY.

2011A01660 T01314   30  S 19-1323. EQUIPMENT TESTING AND CERTIFICATION.
2011A01660 T01315   31    (1) PROHIBITIONS AND REQUIREMENTS. THE PROVISIONS OF THIS  SUBDIVISION
2011A01660 T01316   32  SHALL  BE  EFFECTIVE SIXTY DAYS AFTER THE DATE THAT THE FIRST QUALIFYING
2011A01660 T01317   33  TESTING PROGRAM IS APPROVED BY THE DEPARTMENT OR ITS AGENT.
2011A01660 T01318   34    (A) ONLY THE FOLLOWING KINDS OF DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT  ARE  PERMITTED
2011A01660 T01319   35  TO  BE  INSTALLED IN PERC DRY CLEANING FACILITIES SUBJECT TO THIS TITLE:
2011A01660 T01320   36  NEW CLOSED LOOP DRY CLEANING MACHINES; CONVERTED DRY CLEANING  MACHINES;
2011A01660 T01321   37  DOOR  FAN  SYSTEMS;  OR, ADD-ON SECONDARY CONTROL SYSTEMS WHICH MEET THE
2011A01660 T01322   38  DESIGN AND  PERFORMANCE  STANDARDS  AND  TESTING  REQUIREMENTS  OF  THIS
2011A01660 T01323   39  SECTION.  UNLESS  OTHERWISE  SPECIFIED  IN  THIS TITLE, THE DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T01324   40  EQUIPMENT AS MANUFACTURED AND INSTALLED MUST COMPLY IN ALL RESPECTS WITH
2011A01660 T01325   41  THE UNIT UPON WHICH CERTIFICATION BY THE DEPARTMENT  OR  ITS  AGENT  WAS
2011A01660 T01326   42  BASED.
2011A01660 T01327   43    (B)  ANY  MANUFACTURER  OR  VENDOR OF ANY NEW CLOSED LOOP DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T01328   44  EQUIPMENT THAT IS TO BE INSTALLED IN AND USED BY A DRY CLEANING FACILITY
2011A01660 T01329   45  IN NEW YORK STATE MUST APPLY FOR  AND  RECEIVE  CERTIFICATION  FROM  THE
2011A01660 T01330   46  DEPARTMENT  OR ITS AGENT THAT THE EQUIPMENT TO BE INSTALLED AND OPERATED
2011A01660 T01331   47  COMPLIES IN ALL RESPECTS WITH  THE  PERFORMANCE  STANDARDS  AND  TESTING
2011A01660 T01332   48  REQUIREMENTS  OF  THIS  TITLE. SUCH CERTIFICATION MUST INCLUDE OPERATING
2011A01660 T01333   49  PARAMETERS UNDER WHICH THE  EQUIPMENT  WAS  TESTED  TO  RECEIVE  CERTIF-
2011A01660 T01334   50  ICATION.
2011A01660 T01335   51    (C) IT IS UNLAWFUL FOR ANY PERSON TO SELL, OFFER FOR SALE, CAUSE TO BE
2011A01660 T01336   52  OFFERED FOR SALE, LEASE OR REPRESENT NEW CLOSED LOOP DRY CLEANING EQUIP-
2011A01660 T01337   53  MENT  OR  ANY OTHER MACHINE OR SYSTEM DESCRIBED IN PARAGRAPH (A) OF THIS
2011A01660 T01338   54  SUBDIVISION AS ONE WHICH CAN BE USED BY A DRY CLEANING FACILITY  IN  NEW
2011A01660 T01339   55  YORK STATE UNLESS IT HAS BEEN CERTIFIED BY THE DEPARTMENT OR ITS AGENT.
2011A01660 T01340
2011A01660 T01341       A. 1660                            24
2011A01660 T01342
2011A01660 T01343    1    (D)  THE  CONTRACT  OF SALE, LEASE, OR USE BETWEEN THE MANUFACTURER OR
2011A01660 T01344    2  VENDOR AND DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT USER MUST CONTAIN,  AT  A  MINIMUM,  A
2011A01660 T01345    3  PROVISION  STATING  THAT  THE MANUFACTURER OR VENDOR MUST, UPON REQUEST,
2011A01660 T01346    4  PROVIDE THE USER WITH A COPY OF THE CERTIFICATION OF  THE  EQUIPMENT  BY
2011A01660 T01347    5  THE DEPARTMENT OR ITS AGENT, AS REQUIRED IN THIS TITLE.

2011A01660 T01349    7  THE DEPARTMENT OF ANY GENERIC DESIGN OR FUNCTIONAL DEFECT DISCOVERED  IN
2011A01660 T01350    8  THE  EQUIPMENT. SUCH NOTICE MUST INCLUDE A DETAILED PLAN OF THE MANUFAC-
2011A01660 T01351    9  TURER'S OR VENDOR'S REMEDY.
2011A01660 T01352   10    (F) AFTER THE CERTIFIED DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT HAS BEEN  INSTALLED  AT
2011A01660 T01353   11  THE  USER'S  FACILITY, THE MANUFACTURER OR MANUFACTURER'S REPRESENTATIVE
2011A01660 T01354   12  MUST SUPPLY AT LEAST A TWO-DAY TRAINING  SESSION  TO  THE  PURCHASER  OR
2011A01660 T01355   13  LEASEE.  THE  TRAINING  MUST  INCLUDE INSTRUCTION ON HOW TO MAINTAIN AND
2011A01660 T01356   14  OPERATE THE DRY CLEANING MACHINE. THIS REQUIREMENT  DOES  NOT  APPLY  TO
2011A01660 T01357   15  ADD-ON DOOR FAN SYSTEMS DESIGNED TO CAPTURE DRUM VAPORS WHEN THE DOOR IS
2011A01660 T01358   16  OPEN.
2011A01660 T01359   17    (2)  EQUIPMENT TESTING. FOR A GIVEN DESIGN, A SINGLE TEST PROGRAM MUST
2011A01660 T01360   18  BE CONDUCTED IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE  FOLLOWING  PROCEDURES:  THE  PERSON
2011A01660 T01361   19  CONDUCTING  THE  TEST  PROGRAM  MUST  PREPARE  A  WRITTEN TEST PLAN THAT
2011A01660 T01362   20  DESCRIBES, IN DETAIL, THE DRY CLEANING MACHINE AND CONTROL SYSTEMS BEING
2011A01660 T01363   21  TESTED, THE TEST PROTOCOL, AND TEST METHODS.
2011A01660 T01364   22    (A) TEST PROGRAM AND  SCOPE.    A  MINIMUM  OF  THREE  TESTS  MUST  BE
2011A01660 T01365   23  CONDUCTED  FOR  EACH  TEST  PROGRAM  ON EACH CONTROL SYSTEM DESIGN.  ALL
2011A01660 T01366   24  TESTS FOR A SINGLE TEST PROGRAM MUST BE CONDUCTED ON A SINGLE DRY CLEAN-
2011A01660 T01367   25  ING MACHINE.
2011A01660 T01368   26    (B) TEST CONDITIONS.  TESTING MUST BE CONDUCTED UNDER NORMAL OPERATING
2011A01660 T01369   27  CONDITIONS, UNLESS OTHERWISE SPECIFIED.
2011A01660 T01370   28    (I) FOR PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEMS AND SECONDARY  CONTROL  SYSTEMS,  EACH
2011A01660 T01371   29  TEST MUST BE CONDUCTED DURING THE CLEANING OF ONE LOAD OF MATERIALS.
2011A01660 T01372   30    (A)  THE MACHINE MUST BE FILLED TO NO LESS THAN ONE HUNDRED PERCENT OF
2011A01660 T01373   31  ITS CAPACITY WITH ARTICLES FOR EACH TEST.  AT LEAST SEVENTY  PERCENT  OF
2011A01660 T01374   32  THE LOAD TO BE CLEANED MUST BE WOOL OR PADDED MATERIAL.
2011A01660 T01375   33    (B) THE WEIGHT OF ARTICLES MUST BE RECORDED FOR EACH TEST.
2011A01660 T01376   34    (II) A PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEM MUST BE TESTED ON A CLOSED-LOOP MACHINE,
2011A01660 T01377   35  OR A CONVERTED MACHINE, WITHOUT A SECONDARY CONTROL SYSTEM.
2011A01660 T01378   36    (III)  A  SECONDARY  CONTROL  SYSTEM  MUST  BE TESTED ON A CLOSED-LOOP
2011A01660 T01379   37  MACHINE.
2011A01660 T01380   38    (A) AN INTEGRAL SECONDARY CONTROL  SYSTEM  MUST  BE  TESTED  WITH  THE
2011A01660 T01381   39  PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEM OPERATING NORMALLY.
2011A01660 T01382   40    (B) AN ADD-ON SECONDARY CONTROL SYSTEM MUST BE TESTED INDEPENDENT OF A
2011A01660 T01383   41  PRIMARY  CONTROL  SYSTEM  AND THE INITIAL PERC CONCENTRATION IN THE DRUM
2011A01660 T01384   42  MUST BE 8600 PPM OR GREATER.
2011A01660 T01385   43    (C) TEST METHOD.   EQUIPMENT MUST BE TESTED  IN  ACCORDANCE  WITH  THE
2011A01660 T01386   44  FOLLOWING  METHODS.    FOR PRIMARY CONTROL SYSTEMS AND SECONDARY CONTROL
2011A01660 T00000.SO DOC A 1660                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01660 T01387   45  SYSTEMS:
2011A01660 T01388   46    (I) THE TEMPERATURE OF THE AIR  IN  THE  DRUM  MUST  BE  MEASURED  AND
2011A01660 T01389   47  RECORDED  CONTINUOUSLY  DURING  THE  ENTIRE  DRYING CYCLE, INCLUDING THE
2011A01660 T01390   48  OPERATION OF THE SECONDARY CONTROL SYSTEM.
2011A01660 T01391   49    (II) SAMPLING MUST BE CONDUCTED AS FOLLOWS:
2011A01660 T01392   50    (A)  FOR  PRIMARY  CONTROL  SYSTEMS  AND  INTEGRAL  SECONDARY  CONTROL
2011A01660 T01393   51  SYSTEMS,  SAMPLING  MUST  BEGIN  AT  THE  END OF THE DRYING CYCLE AND BE
2011A01660 T01394   52  COMPLETED WITHIN FIVE MINUTES.
2011A01660 T01395   53    (B) FOR ADD-ON SECONDARY CONTROL SYSTEMS, SAMPLING MUST BE  DONE  WHEN
2011A01660 T01396   54  THE  CONCENTRATION  OF  PERC  IS  8600 PPM OR GREATER AND AGAIN WHEN THE
2011A01660 T01397   55  CONCENTRATION REACHES 300 PPM OR LESS.
2011A01660 T01398
2011A01660 T01399       A. 1660                            25

2011A01660 T01401    1    (C) SAMPLING MUST BE COMPLETED PRIOR TO THE  OPENING  OF  THE  MACHINE
2011A01660 T01402    2  DOOR AND ACTIVATION OF ANY FUGITIVE CONTROL SYSTEM.

2011A01660 T01463    4  S  19-1325.  DRY CLEANING OWNER/MANAGER, OPERATOR AND INSPECTOR TRAINING
2011A01660 T01464    5               AND CERTIFICATION.
2011A01660 T01465    6    (1) NO DRY CLEANING FACILITY SUBJECT TO THIS TITLE SHALL BE  PERMITTED
2011A01660 T01466    7  TO  OPERATE  UNLESS  SAID  FACILITY IS UNDER THE SUPERVISION OF A PERSON
2011A01660 T01467    8  POSSESSING A DRY  CLEANING  OWNER/MANAGER  CERTIFICATION;  AND  THE  DRY
2011A01660 T01468    9  CLEANING MACHINE IS OPERATED BY A PERSON HOLDING A DRY CLEANING OPERATOR
2011A01660 T01469   10  CERTIFICATION.    EXCEPT FOR THE CONDITIONS ESTABLISHED IN SUBDIVISION 2
2011A01660 T01470   11  OF THIS SECTION, IT IS UNLAWFUL FOR ANY PERSON TO OPERATE A DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T01471   12  FACILITY SUBJECT TO THIS TITLE UNLESS:
2011A01660 T01472   13    (A) THE FACILITY MANAGER AND/OR OWNER HAS  A  CURRENT  AND  VALID  DRY
2011A01660 T01473   14  CLEANING OWNER/MANAGER CERTIFICATION; AND
2011A01660 T01474   15    (B)  THE  PERSON  OPERATING THE DRY CLEANING MACHINE HAS A CURRENT AND
2011A01660 T01475   16  VALID DRY CLEANING OPERATOR CERTIFICATION.
2011A01660 T01476   17    (2) IN THE EVENT THAT AN UNFORESEEN/UNPREDICTABLE SITUATION PREVENTS A
2011A01660 T01477   18  DRY CLEANING FACILITY FROM HAVING A CERTIFIED OPERATOR OPERATING THE DRY
2011A01660 T01478   19  CLEANING EQUIPMENT, THE OWNER/MANAGER SHALL BE ALLOWED TO CONTINUE OPER-
2011A01660 T01479   20  ATION OF THE DRY CLEANING MACHINE WITH A NON-CERTIFIED  OPERATOR  FOR  A
2011A01660 T01480   21  PERIOD  NOT TO EXCEED THREE DAYS PER OCCURRENCE.  UNDER NO CIRCUMSTANCES
2011A01660 T01481   22  MAY AN UNCERTIFIED OPERATOR OPERATE DRY CLEANING EQUIPMENT AT ANY FACIL-
2011A01660 T01482   23  ITY FOR A TOTAL OF MORE THAN TEN DAYS IN ANY CALENDAR YEAR.  IF, THE USE
2011A01660 T01483   24  OF AN UNCERTIFIED OPERATOR WOULD CAUSE NONPERFORMANCE OF REQUIRED  MAIN-
2011A01660 T01484   25  TENANCE AND LEAK DETECTION, THE FACILITY MUST SUSPEND DRY CLEANING OPER-
2011A01660 T01485   26  ATIONS  UNTIL  A  CERTIFIED OPERATOR IS AVAILABLE.   THE PURPOSE OF THIS
2011A01660 T00000.SO DOC A 1660                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01660 T01486   27  PROVISION IS TO ACCOMMODATE EMERGENCY OR UNFORESEEN EXTENUATING  CIRCUM-
2011A01660 T01487   28  STANCES  AND  MUST  NOT  BE  USED  TO  COVER  ROUTINE SITUATIONS SUCH AS
2011A01660 T01488   29  VACATIONS, OR OTHER SCHEDULED ABSENCES.
2011A01660 T01489   30    (3) A DRY CLEANING OWNER/MANAGER CERTIFICATION MAY BE  ISSUED  BY  ANY
2011A01660 T01490   31  ORGANIZATION  THAT OFFERS A TRAINING PROGRAM (INCLUDING REFRESHER COURS-
2011A01660 T01491   32  ES) APPROVED BY THE DEPARTMENT THAT INCLUDES, BUT IS NOT LIMITED TO, THE
2011A01660 T01492   33  FOLLOWING ELEMENTS:
2011A01660 T01493   34    (A) COURSE TOPICS:
2011A01660 T01494   35    (I) THE HISTORY OF DRY CLEANING AND WET CLEANING TECHNIQUES  INCLUDING
2011A01660 T01495   36  THE APPROPRIATE USE OF EACH;
2011A01660 T01496   37    (II) ALTERNATIVES TO PERC, INCLUDING GREATER USE OF WET CLEANING;
2011A01660 T01497   38    (III) THE CHARACTERISTICS AND ENVIRONMENTAL EFFECTS OF PERC;
2011A01660 T01498   39    (IV) THE HEALTH IMPACTS OF PERC;

2011A01660 T01501   42  RECORDKEEPING AND REPORTING REQUIREMENTS, INCLUDING  THE  ADMINISTRATION
2011A01660 T01502   43  AND  IMPLEMENTATION  OF APPROPRIATE STATE AND FEDERAL LABOR, HEALTH, AND

2011A01660 T01608   33    (2)  ANY  PERSON  WHO  OWNS AN EXISTING FACILITY SUBJECT TO THIS TITLE
2011A01660 T01609   34  MUST TAKE ONE OR MORE OF THE FOLLOWING ACTIONS WITHIN THE  TIME  PERIODS

2011A01660 T01642    8  S 19-1329. COMPLIANCE INSPECTIONS.
2011A01660 T01643    9    (1) STAND-ALONG DRY CLEANING FACILITIES MUST  BE  INSPECTED  AT  LEAST
2011A01660 T01644   10  ANNUALLY,  AND  MIXED-USE  FACILITIES MUST BE INSPECTED ACCORDING TO THE
2011A01660 T01645   11  FOLLOWING SCHEDULE:
2011A01660 T01646   12    (A) AT LEAST TWICE ANNUALLY WHERE ANY TRANSFER  OR  DRY-TO-DRY  VENTED
2011A01660 T01647   13  EQUIPMENT IS OPERATED; OR
2011A01660 T01648   14    (B) AT LEAST ANNUALLY WHERE ONLY NON-VENTED EQUIPMENT IS OPERATED.
2011A01660 T01649   15    (2) SUCH INSPECTIONS MUST BE PERFORMED BY AN INSPECTOR REGISTERED WITH
2011A01660 T01650   16  THE  DEPARTMENT  OR  BY AN INDIVIDUAL WORKING UNDER THE SUPERVISION OF A
2011A01660 T01651   17  REGISTERED INSPECTOR.
2011A01660 T01652   18    (3) ALL REGISTERED INSPECTORS MUST MEET THE REQUIREMENTS OF PARAGRAPHS
2011A01660 T01653   19  (A), (B) AND (C) OF THIS SUBDIVISION. ALL INDIVIDUALS WORKING UNDER  THE
2011A01660 T01654   20  SUPERVISION  OF  A  REGISTERED  INSPECTOR  MUST MEET THE REQUIREMENTS OF
2011A01660 T01655   21  PARAGRAPHS (B) AND (C) OF THIS SUBDIVISION.
2011A01660 T01656   22    (A) THE INSPECTOR MUST BE ONE OF THE FOLLOWING:
2011A01660 T01657   23    (I) A LICENSED PROFESSIONAL ENGINEER;
2011A01660 T01658   24    (II) A REGISTERED ARCHITECT; OR
2011A01660 T01659   25    (III) A CERTIFIED INDUSTRIAL HYGIENIST.
2011A01660 T01660   26    (B) MUST POSSESS A DRY CLEANER OWNER/MANAGER CERTIFICATION IN  ACCORD-
2011A01660 T01661   27  ANCE  WITH  SECTION 19-1325 OF THIS TITLE AND COMPLETE OTHER APPROPRIATE
2011A01660 T01662   28  TRAINING  AS  SPECIFIED  BY  THE  DEPARTMENT  ON   TOPICS   RELATED   TO
2011A01660 T01663   29  INSPECTIONS.
2011A01660 T01664   30    (C)  MUST  NOT  BE  ENGAGED  IN THE SALES OR MARKETING OF DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T01665   31  EQUIPMENT. MUST NOT BE ENGAGED IN PROVIDING SERVICES TO THE DRY CLEANING
2011A01660 T01666   32  INDUSTRY. EMPLOYEES OF TRADE ASSOCIATIONS MAY NOT  CONDUCT  INSPECTIONS,
2011A01660 T01667   33  BUT  TRADE  ASSOCIATIONS  MAY SOLICIT BIDS FOR PERFORMING INSPECTIONS ON
2011A01660 T01668   34  BEHALF OF THEIR MEMBERS.
2011A01660 T01669   35    (4) THE DEPARTMENT MUST BE NOTIFIED OF ALL INSPECTIONS, IN WRITING  AT
2011A01660 T01670   36  LEAST  SEVEN  DAYS  PRIOR  TO  INSPECTION,  IN  A FORM ACCEPTABLE TO THE
2011A01660 T01671   37  DEPARTMENT, BY THE REGISTERED INSPECTOR.
2011A01660 T01672   38    (5) INSPECTIONS MUST BE CONDUCTED IN ACCORDANCE WITH PROTOCOLS  SPECI-
2011A01660 T01673   39  FIED  BY THE DEPARTMENT, USING AN INSPECTION REPORTING FORM SPECIFIED BY
2011A01660 T01674   40  THE DEPARTMENT.
2011A01660 T01675   41    (6) ANALYSIS OF AIR SAMPLES COLLECTED BY PASSIVE SAMPLING  DEVICES  OR
2011A01660 T01676   42  THE  EQUIVALENT MUST BE CONDUCTED BY A LABORATORY CERTIFIED BY THE ENVI-
2011A01660 T01677   43  RONMENTAL LABORATORY APPROVAL PROGRAM  (ELAP)  OF  THE  NEW  YORK  STATE
2011A01660 T01678   44  DEPARTMENT OF HEALTH.
2011A01660 T01679   45    (7)  THE  INSPECTION SHALL VERIFY THAT THE DEPARTMENT NOTICE IS POSTED
2011A01660 T01680   46  IN A CONSPICUOUS LOCATION IN THE FACILITY.
2011A01660 T01681   47    (8) AFTER THE INSPECTION IS COMPLETED, THE REGISTERED  INSPECTOR  MUST
2011A01660 T01682   48  PROVIDE  A  COMPLETED INSPECTION REPORTING FORM TO THE DEPARTMENT AND TO
2011A01660 T01683   49  THE FACILITY OWNER WITHIN FORTY-FIVE DAYS OF THE INSPECTION.

2011A01660 T01684   50    (9) FAILURE OF THE REGISTERED  INSPECTOR  TO  COMPLY  WITH  THE  ABOVE
2011A01660 T01685   51  REQUIREMENTS  MAY RESULT IN THE REMOVAL OF THE REGISTERED INSPECTOR FROM
2011A01660 T01686   52  THE DEPARTMENT'S LIST OF REGISTERED INSPECTORS.

2011A01660 T01716   23  CONSISTENT WITH SECTIONS 19-1311 AND 19-1313 OF THIS TITLE; AND,
2011A01660 T01717   24    (E) DOCUMENTATION ON SOLVENT MILEAGE (POUNDS OF ARTICLES  CLEANED  PER
2011A01660 T01718   25  GALLON  OF  SOLVENT ADDED) ACHIEVED WITH AND WITHOUT USE OF THE ALTERNA-
2011A01660 T01719   26  TIVE EMISSION CONTROL  TECHNOLOGY.  SOLVENT  MILEAGE  DATA  MUST  BE  OF
2011A01660 T01720   27  CONTINUOUS  DURATION  FOR  AT  LEAST  ONE YEAR UNDER THE CONDITIONS OF A
2011A01660 T01721   28  TYPICAL DRY CLEANING OPERATION. THIS INFORMATION ON SOLVENT MILEAGE MUST
2011A01660 T01722   29  BE ACCOMPANIED BY INFORMATION ON THE DESIGN,  CONFIGURATION,  OPERATION,
2011A01660 T01723   30  AND  MAINTENANCE  OF  THE  SPECIFIC  DRY  CLEANING SYSTEM FROM WHICH THE
2011A01660 T01724   31  SOLVENT MILEAGE INFORMATION WAS OBTAINED.
2011A01660 T01725   32    (2) INFORMATION INDICATING THE LEVEL OF EMISSIONS  REQUIRED  IN  PARA-
2011A01660 T01726   33  GRAPH  (B)  OF  SUBDIVISION  ONE  OF  THIS SECTION MUST ACHIEVE EMISSION
2011A01660 T01727   34  REDUCTIONS EQUAL TO OR LESS THAN THOSE STATED IN SECTION 19-1309 OF THIS
2011A01660 T01728   35  TITLE FOR COMPARATIVE TECHNOLOGY.
2011A01660 T01729   36    (3) FOR THE PURPOSE OF DETERMINING EQUIVALENCY OF CONTROL OF EMISSIONS
2011A01660 T01730   37  TO THOSE REQUIRED UNDER THIS TITLE, THE DEPARTMENT SHALL EVALUATE WHETH-
2011A01660 T01731   38  ER THE ALTERNATIVE CONTROL TECHNOLOGY HAS BEEN DEMONSTRATED  ADEQUATELY.
2011A01660 T01732   39  IF  THE  DEMONSTRATION  IS ADEQUATE, THE ALTERNATIVE TECHNOLOGY SHALL BE
2011A01660 T01733   40  ELIGIBLE FOR CERTIFICATION.
2011A01660 T01734   41    (4) ANY DECISION MADE BY THE DEPARTMENT IN  ACCORDANCE  WITH  SUBDIVI-
2011A01660 T01735   42  SIONS  1, 2 AND 3 OF THIS SECTION IS CONTINGENT UPON REVIEW AND APPROVAL
2011A01660 T01736   43  BY EPA.
2011A01660 T01737   44  S 19-1333. POSTING NOTICE.
2011A01660 T01738   45    (1) EVERY PERC-BASED DRY CLEANING FACILITY SHALL BE REQUIRED TO PROMI-
2011A01660 T01739   46  NENTLY POST A NOTICE PREPARED  AND  SUPPLIED  BY  THE  DEPARTMENT  IN  A
2011A01660 T01740   47  CONSPICUOUS  LOCATION  IN  THE  DRY  CLEANING  FACILITY WHICH IS READILY
2011A01660 T01741   48  ACCESSIBLE TO ALL BUILDING  TENANTS  AND  CUSTOMERS.  THE  NOTICE  SHALL
2011A01660 T01742   49  CONTAIN  THE FOLLOWING STATEMENTS AND INFORMATION, PRINTED IN LETTERS AT
2011A01660 T01743   50  LEAST 3/8" OR LARGER IN SIZE:
2011A01660 T01744   51    (A) "THIS DRY CLEANING FACILITY USES THE CHEMICAL COMMONLY CALLED PERC
2011A01660 T01745   52  (ALSO CALLED  TETRACHLORETHENE,  TETRACHLOROETHYLENE  OR  PERCHLOROETHY-
2011A01660 T01746   53  LENE)."
2011A01660 T01747   54    (B)  "THE FOLLOWING POTENTIAL HEALTH EFFECTS ARE ASSOCIATED WITH EXPO-
2011A01660 T01748   55  SURE TO PERC EMISSIONS:
2011A01660 T01749
2011A01660 T01750       A. 1660                            31
2011A01660 T01751
2011A01660 T01752    1    (I) PERC HAS BEEN CLASSIFIED BY THE INTERNATIONAL AGENCY FOR  RESEARCH
2011A01660 T01753    2  ON  CANCER AS A 'PROBABLE HUMAN CARCINOGEN', WHICH MEANS THERE ARE RELI-
2011A01660 T01754    3  ABLE STUDIES OF HUMAN POPULATIONS EXPOSED TO  PERC  THAT  SHOW  ELEVATED
2011A01660 T01755    4  CANCER RATES.
2011A01660 T01756    5    (II)  EXPOSURE  TO PERC CAUSES DAMAGE TO THE LIVER, KIDNEY AND CENTRAL
2011A01660 T01757    6  NERVOUS SYSTEM.
2011A01660 T01758    7    (III) PERC MAY BE ABSORBED INTO THE BODY AFTER  INGESTION,  INHALATION
2011A01660 T01759    8  OR CONTACT WITH THE SKIN.
2011A01660 T01760    9    (IV) PERC IS CLASSIFIED BY THE U.S. ENVIRONMENTAL PROTECTION AGENCY AS
2011A01660 T01761   10  A HAZARDOUS AIR POLLUTANT.
2011A01660 T01762   11    (C) "YOU SHOULD CONTACT THE NEW YORK STATE DEPARTMENT OF ENVIRONMENTAL
2011A01660 T01763   12  CONSERVATION  IF YOU SMELL CHEMICAL ODORS OR SEE LIQUID LEAKING FROM THE
2011A01660 T01764   13  DRY CLEANING OPERATIONS AT (INCLUDE TELEPHONE NUMBER)."
2011A01660 T01765   14    (D)  "YOU  MAY  REQUEST  INFORMATION  FROM  THIS  DRY  CLEANER   ABOUT
2011A01660 T01766   15  INSPECTIONS  THAT  MAY  HAVE  BEEN CONDUCTED AT THIS FACILITY, INCLUDING
2011A01660 T01767   16  INDOOR AIR TESTING."
2011A01660 T01768   17    (E) NAME OF DRY CLEANING FACILITY, DEPARTMENT PERMIT  OR  REGISTRATION
2011A01660 T01769   18  NUMBER,  FACILITY  ADDRESS,  FACILITY OWNER, EMERGENCY CONTACT TELEPHONE
2011A01660 T01770   19  NUMBER.
2011A01660 T01771   20    (2) THE SIGN MUST BE AT LEAST ELEVEN INCHES  BY  SEVENTEEN  INCHES  IN
2011A01660 T01772   21  SIZE; AND YELLOW WITH BLACK LETTERING.
2011A01660 T01773   22  S 19-1335. SEVERABILITY.
2011A01660 T01774   23    IF  ANY  PROVISION  OF  THIS TITLE OR ITS APPLICATION TO ANY PERSON OR
2011A01660 T01775   24  CIRCUMSTANCE IS HELD INVALID, THE  REMAINDER  OF  THIS  TITLE,  AND  THE
2011A01660 T01776   25  APPLICATION  OF THOSE PROVISIONS TO PERSONS OTHER THAN THOSE TO WHICH IT
2011A01660 T01777   26  IS HELD INVALID, SHALL NOT BE AFFECTED THEREBY.
2011A01660 T01778   27    S 2. The department of  environmental  conservation  shall  take  such
2011A01660 T01779   28  actions as are necessary and appropriate to have perc-based dry cleaning
2011A01660 T01780   29  facilities located in residential buildings phased out within five years
2011A01660 T01781   30  of the effective date of this act.

2011S01611 T00022
2011S01611 T00023    1    Section 1. Subsection (i) of section 3216  of  the  insurance  law  is
2011S01611 T00024    2  amended by adding a new paragraph 28 to read as follows:
2011S01611 T00025    3    (28)  (A) EVERY POLICY WHICH PROVIDES FOR SURGICAL OR MEDICAL COVERAGE
2011S01611 T00026    4  OR IN-PATIENT HOSPITAL CARE AS  WELL  AS  NON-HEALTH  RELATED  SERVICES,
2011S01611 T00027    5  SHALL  MAKE  AVAILABLE,  WHEN REQUESTED BY THE CONTRACT HOLDER, COVERAGE
2011S01611 T00028    6  FOR OUT-PATIENT TREATMENT OF ALZHEIMER'S OR RELATED DISEASES.
2011S01611 T00029    7    (B) FOR THE PURPOSES OF THIS PARAGRAPH, THE FOLLOWING TERMS SHALL HAVE
2011S01611 T00030    8  THE FOLLOWING MEANINGS:
2011S01611 T00031    9    (I) "NON-HEALTH RELATED SERVICES"  MEANS  THOSE  OUT-PATIENT  SERVICES
2011S01611 T00032   10  WHICH  MEET  THE CARE AND BEHAVIORAL NEEDS OF THE PATIENT, INCLUDING BUT
2011S01611 T00033   11  NOT LIMITED TO CRISIS  INTERVENTION,  ADULT  DAY  CARE,  HOME  CARE  AND
2011S01611 T00034   12  RESPITE CARE.
2011S01611 T00035   13    (II)  "CARE  AND BEHAVIORAL NEEDS OF THE PATIENT" MEANS THE MANIFESTA-
2011S01611 T00036   14  TION OF SYMPTOMS WHICH MAY INCLUDE BUT NOT LIMITED TO MEMORY LOSS, APHA-
2011S01611 T00037   15  SIA (COMMUNICATION DISORDER), BECOMING LOST  OR  DISORIENTED,  CONFUSION
2011S01611 T00038   16  AND AGITATION WITH THE POTENTIAL FOR COMBATIVENESS AND INCONTINENCE.
2011S01611 T00039   17    (III)  "ALZHEIMER'S  OR RELATED DISEASES" MEANS ANY OF THOSE IRREVERS-
2011S01611 T00040   18  IBLE BRAIN DISORDERS WHICH RESULT IN  THE  SYMPTOMS  DESCRIBED  IN  THIS
2011S01611 T00041   19  PARAGRAPH  BUT  NOT  LIMITED  TO MULTI-INFARCT DEMENTIAS AND PARKINSON'S
2011S01611 T00042   20  DISEASE.

2011A01652 T00085   31  LABORER FOR RELIGIOUS WORSHIP.

2011A01652 T00319   30  exclusions from the term "employee" contained in this subdivision  shall

2011A01652 T00321   32  volunteer at a recreational or amusement event run by  a  business  that

2011A01652 T00323   34  than eight consecutive days and no more than one such  event  concerning

2011A01652 T00325   36  such volunteer shall be at least eighteen years of age. A business seek-

2011A01652 T00330   41  signed and dated by a representative of the business and  the  volunteer
2011A01652 T00331   42  and kept on file by the business for thirty-six months.

2011A01653 T00045   12  SUGAR, AND SHALL INCLUDE THE OPERATION AND MAINTENANCE OF FARM EQUIPMENT
2011A01653 T00046   13  AND IMPROVEMENT OR MAINTENANCE  OF  FARM  WATER  USE  AREAS,  AND  SHALL
2011A01653 T00047   14  INCLUDE THE PLANTING, DRYING, PACKAGING OR OTHER PROCESSING OF ANY AGRI-

2011A01653 T00203   31  icates  issued by the commissioner, at such wages lower than the minimum
2011A01653 T00204   32  wage established by this  article  and  for  such  period  as  shall  be
2011A01653 T00205   33  prescribed in such regulations.
