2011A01653 T00235    4    S 9. The labor law is amended by adding a new section 704-b to read as
2011A01653 T00236    5  follows:
2011A01653 T00237    6    S  704-B.  UNFAIR LABOR PRACTICES; AGRICULTURE. 1. IT IS THE POLICY OF
2011A01653 T00238    7  THE STATE TO PROTECT THE RIGHTS OF FARM LABORERS WITHOUT CAUSING IMMEDI-
2011A01653 T00239    8  ATE AND IRREPARABLE HARM TO EMPLOYERS. IN RECOGNITION  OF  THE  NEED  TO
2011A01653 T00240    9  AVOID  INTERRUPTION OF THE AGRICULTURAL PRODUCTION OF CROPS WITH A SHORT
2011A01653 T00241   10  PEAK HARVEST SEASON, THIS POLICY IS  BEST  ACHIEVED  BY  PROVIDING  FARM
2011A01653 T00242   11  EMPLOYERS  AND  THEIR  EMPLOYEES WITH A SHORT TEMPORARY PERIOD TO SETTLE
2011A01653 T00243   12  THEIR LABOR DISPUTE WITHOUT CAUSING IMMEDIATE OR IRREPARABLE HARM TO THE
2011A01653 T00244   13  EMPLOYER.
2011A01653 T00245   14    2. DEFINITIONS. WHEN USED IN THIS SECTION THE TERMS:
2011A01653 T00246   15    (A) "SHORT PEAK HARVEST SEASON" MEANS THE PERIOD FOR FRUITS AND  VEGE-
2011A01653 T00247   16  TABLES  THAT  HAVE  A  MAXIMUM  HARVEST PERIOD OF NO MORE THAN SIX WEEKS
2011A01653 T00248   17  DURING WHICH SUCH AGRICULTURAL PRODUCT IS HARVESTED FOR SALE, AS  DETER-
2011A01653 T00249   18  MINED BY THE DEPARTMENT OF AGRICULTURE AND MARKETS.
2011A01653 T00250   19    (B)  "WORK STOPPAGE" MEANS ANY STRIKE, OR CONCERTED CESSATION OR SLOW-
2011A01653 T00251   20  DOWN OF WORK BY EMPLOYEES.
2011A01653 T00252   21    (C) "LOCKOUT" MEANS A WORK STOPPAGE DURING WHICH AN EMPLOYER  PREVENTS
2011A01653 T00253   22  EMPLOYEES FROM WORKING.
2011A01653 T00254   23    3. IN THE EVENT THAT THE BOARD AND ITS EMPLOYEES RECEIVE NOTICE THAT A
2011A01653 T00255   24  LABOR DISPUTE HAS ARISEN BETWEEN A FARM EMPLOYER THAT WILL OR MAY RESULT
2011A01653 T00256   25  IN  A  WORK  STOPPAGE  OR  LOCKOUT, THE BOARD SHALL IMMEDIATELY INITIATE
2011A01653 T00257   26  SETTLEMENT PROCEEDINGS UNDER SECTION SEVEN HUNDRED TWO-A OF  THIS  ARTI-
2011A01653 T00258   27  CLE.
2011A01653 T00259   28    (A)  AFTER THE INITIATION OF SETTLEMENT PROCEEDINGS, ANY WORK STOPPAGE
2011A01653 T00260   29  OR LOCKOUT SHALL CEASE FOR A PERIOD OF NOT MORE THAN TWENTY-ONE DAYS  IF
2011A01653 T00261   30  BOTH OF THE FOLLOWING CIRCUMSTANCES EXIST:
2011A01653 T00262   31    (I)  THE  WORK  STOPPAGE OR LOCKOUT OCCURS DURING A SHORT PEAK HARVEST
2011A01653 T00263   32  SEASON; AND
2011A01653 T00264   33    (II) THE WORK STOPPAGE OR LOCKOUT WILL CAUSE IMMEDIATE AND IRREPARABLE
2011A01653 T00265   34  INJURY, LOSS OR DAMAGE TO THE EMPLOYER.
2011A01653 T00266   35    (B) DURING SUCH TWENTY-ONE DAY PERIOD, BOTH PARTIES SHALL  ENTER  INTO
2011A01653 T00267   36  GOOD  FAITH NEGOTIATIONS TO SETTLE THE LABOR DISPUTE, WHICH PERIOD SHALL
2011A01653 T00268   37  BE REFERRED TO AS A COOLING OFF PERIOD.
2011A01653 T00269   38    (C) THE BOARD SHALL CONDUCT AN IMMEDIATE  AND  EXPEDITED  FACT-FINDING
2011A01653 T00270   39  HEARING  TO  DETERMINE  WHETHER THE CIRCUMSTANCES UNDER PARAGRAPH (A) OF
2011A01653 T00271   40  THIS SUBDIVISION EXIST. EACH PARTY SHALL HAVE THE OPPORTUNITY TO  SUBMIT
2011A01653 T00272   41  WRITTEN  AND ORAL TESTIMONY AT THE HEARING. THE BOARD SHALL NOT BE BOUND
2011A01653 T00273   42  BY TECHNICAL RULES OF EVIDENCE PREVAILING IN COURTS OF LAW OR EQUITY.
2011A01653 T00274   43    (D)  THE  BOARD  SHALL  ISSUE  ITS  DETERMINATION  IN  WRITING  WITHIN
2011A01653 T00275   44  FORTY-EIGHT  HOURS OF THE CONCLUSION OF THE HEARING, WHICH SHALL INCLUDE
2011A01653 T00276   45  FINDINGS OF FACT AND A RATIONALE FOR ITS DETERMINATION. A  COPY  OF  THE
2011A01653 T00277   46  BOARD'S DETERMINATION SHALL BE PROVIDED TO EACH PARTY WITHIN TWENTY-FOUR
2011A01653 T00278   47  HOURS.
2011A01653 T00279   48    (E)  FOR PURPOSES OF THIS SECTION, AN EMPLOYEE WHO IS ABSENT FROM WORK
2011A01653 T00280   49  WITHOUT PERMISSION, OR WHO ABSTAINS WHOLLY OR  IN  PART  FROM  THE  FULL
2011A01653 T00281   50  PERFORMANCE  OF  HIS  OR HER EMPLOYMENT DUTIES WITHOUT PERMISSION ON THE
2011A01653 T00282   51  DATE WHEN A WORK STOPPAGE OR LOCKOUT OCCURS SHALL BE  PRESUMED  TO  HAVE
2011A01653 T00283   52  ENGAGED IN SUCH WORK STOPPAGE OR LOCKOUT.
2011A01653 T00284   53    4. IF EITHER PARTY IS FOUND TO BE IN VIOLATION OF THE BOARD'S DETERMI-
2011A01653 T00285   54  NATION,  THE  BOARD MAY FILE A PETITION WITH THE SUPREME COURT IN ALBANY
2011A01653 T00286   55  COUNTY UPON NOTICE TO ALL PARTIES FOR TEMPORARY INJUNCTIVE  RELIEF.  THE
2011A01653 T00287   56  BOARD  SHALL  NOT  BE  REQUIRED  TO PROVIDE ANY UNDERTAKINGS OR BOND AND
2011A01653 T00288
2011A01653 T00289       A. 1653                             6
2011A01653 T00290
2011A01653 T00291    1  SHALL NOT BE LIABLE FOR  ANY  DAMAGES  OR  COSTS  WHICH  MAY  HAVE  BEEN
2011A01653 T00292    2  SUSTAINED  BY  REASON OF ANY TEMPORARY INJUNCTIVE RELIEF ORDERED. IF THE
2011A01653 T00293    3  BOARD FAILS TO ACT WITHIN TEN DAYS, THE BOARD SHALL BE  DEEMED  TO  HAVE
2011A01653 T00294    4  MADE A FINAL DETERMINATION NOT TO SEEK TEMPORARY INJUNCTIVE RELIEF.

2011A01653 T00297    7    S 719. ADVISORY COMMITTEE ON AGRICULTURAL COLLECTIVE BARGAINING.    1.

2011A01653 T00306   16  THE NEW YORK STATE AMERICAN FEDERATION OF LABOR-CONGRESS  OF  INDUSTRIAL
2011A01653 T00307   17  ORGANIZATIONS,  ONE  UPON  THE  NOMINATION  OF  THE  NEW YORK STATE FARM
2011A01653 T00308   18  BUREAU, AND ONE MEMBER  WITH  EXPERIENCE  AND  EXPERTISE  IN  COLLECTIVE
2011A01653 T00309   19  BARGAINING AND LABOR RELATIONS WHO SHALL BE APPOINTED TO CHAIR THE ADVI-
2011A01653 T00310   20  SORY COMMITTEE.

2011A01653 T00312   22  TO IMPLEMENT  COLLECTIVE  BARGAINING  STRUCTURES  AND  PROCEDURES  WHERE
2011A01653 T00313   23  APPROPRIATE,  AND  TO  FOSTER  LABOR-MANAGEMENT  COOPERATION AND DISPUTE

2011A01653 T00317   27  COLLECTIVE BARGAINING AND LABOR RELATIONS IN FARM  EMPLOYMENT,  AND  THE
2011A01653 T00318   28  UNIQUE  CHARACTERISTICS  OF  THE  AGRICULTURE INDUSTRY INCLUDING BUT NOT
2011A01653 T00319   29  LIMITED TO LENGTH OF HARVEST AND GROWING SEASONS, SEASONAL  FLUCTUATIONS
2011A01653 T00320   30  IN  EMPLOYMENT, ANNUAL SALES, AND IMPORT AND EXPORT CONDITIONS AFFECTING
2011A01653 T00321   31  NEW YORK AGRICULTURE. THE ADVISORY COMMITTEE SHALL REPORT TO THE  GOVER-
2011A01653 T00322   32  NOR,  THE  SPEAKER  OF  THE  ASSEMBLY AND THE TEMPORARY PRESIDENT OF THE
2011A01653 T00323   33  SENATE ON OR BEFORE DECEMBER THIRTY-FIRST, TWO THOUSAND TWELVE.
2011A01653 T00324   34    3. THE MEMBERS OF THE ADVISORY COMMITTEE SHALL RECEIVE NO COMPENSATION
2011A01653 T00325   35  FOR THEIR SERVICES, BUT SHALL BE  ALLOWED  THEIR  ACTUAL  AND  NECESSARY
2011A01653 T00326   36  EXPENSES INCURRED IN THE PERFORMANCE OF THEIR DUTIES.

2011S01613 T00017       AN ACT to amend the banking law,  in  relation  to  refund  anticipation
2011S01613 T00018         loans
2011S01613 T00019
2011S01613 T00020         THE  PEOPLE OF THE STATE OF NEW YORK, REPRESENTED IN SENATE AND ASSEM-
2011S01613 T00021       BLY, DO ENACT AS FOLLOWS:
2011S01613 T00022
2011S01613 T00023    1    Section 1. The banking law is amended by adding a new  section  46  to
2011S01613 T00024    2  read as follows:
2011S01613 T00025    3    S 46. REFUND ANTICIPATION LOANS. 1. AS USED IN THIS SECTION:
2011S01613 T00026    4    (A)  "BORROWER"  MEANS  A PERSON WHO RECEIVES THE PROCEEDS OF A REFUND
2011S01613 T00027    5  ANTICIPATION LOAN;
2011S01613 T00028    6    (B) "FACILITATOR" MEANS A PERSON WHO, INDIVIDUALLY, OR IN  CONJUNCTION
2011S01613 T00029    7  OR  COOPERATION  WITH  ANOTHER PERSON, MAKES A REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN,
2011S01613 T00030    8  PROCESSES, RECEIVES OR ACCEPTS FOR DELIVERY AN APPLICATION FOR A  REFUND
2011S01613 T00031    9  ANTICIPATION LOAN, ISSUES A CHECK IN PAYMENT OF REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN
2011S01613 T00032   10  PROCEEDS,  OR  IN  ANY OTHER MANNER ACTS TO ALLOW THE MAKING OF A REFUND
2011S01613 T00033   11  ANTICIPATION LOAN. THE TERM DOES NOT  INCLUDE  A  BANK,  TRUST  COMPANY,
2011S01613 T00034   12  SAVINGS  BANK,  SAVINGS  AND LOAN ASSOCIATION, CREDIT UNION OR PERSON OR
2011S01613 T00035   13  ENTITY ISSUED A LICENSE UNDER THE PROVISIONS OF  ARTICLE  NINE  OF  THIS
2011S01613 T00036   14  CHAPTER, OPERATING UNDER THE LAWS OF THE UNITED STATES OR THIS STATE, OR
2011S01613 T00037   15  ANY PERSON WHO ACTS SOLELY AS AN INTERMEDIARY AND DOES NOT DEAL WITH THE
2011S01613 T00038   16  PUBLIC IN THE MAKING OF A REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN;
2011S01613 T00039   17    (C)  "REFUND  ANTICIPATION  LOAN"  MEANS  A  LOAN  ARRANGED TO BE PAID
2011S01613 T00040   18  DIRECTLY FROM THE PROCEEDS OF A BORROWER'S INCOME TAX REFUND;
2011S01613 T00041   19    (D) "REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN FEE" MEANS ANY CHARGES,  FEES  OR  OTHER
2011S01613 T00042   20  CONSIDERATION CHARGED OR IMPOSED FOR THE MAKING OF A REFUND ANTICIPATION
2011S01613 T00043   21  LOAN. THE TERM DOES NOT INCLUDE ANY CHARGES, FEES OR OTHER CONSIDERATION
2011S01613 T00044   22  CHARGED  OR  IMPOSED IN THE ORDINARY COURSE OF BUSINESS BY A FACILITATOR
2011S01613 T00045   23  FOR SERVICES THAT DO NOT RESULT IN THE MAKING OF A LOAN  INCLUDING,  BUT
2011S01613 T00046   24  NOT  LIMITED  TO,  FEES  FOR  TAX RETURN PREPARATION SERVICES OR FOR THE
2011S01613 T00047   25  ELECTRONIC FILING OF INCOME TAX RETURNS; AND
2011S01613 T00048
2011S01613 T00049        EXPLANATION--Matter in ITALICS (underscored) is new; matter in brackets
2011S01613 T00050                             [ ] is old law to be omitted.
2011S01613 T00051                                                                  LBD05683-01-1
2011S01613 T00052
2011S01613 T00053       S. 1613                             2
2011S01613 T00054
2011S01613 T00055    1    (E) "ANNUAL PERCENTAGE RATE" SHALL HAVE THE SAME MEANING  AS  PROVIDED
2011S01613 T00056    2  IN PARAGRAPH (B) OF SUBDIVISION ONE OF SECTION SIX-L OF THIS CHAPTER.
2011S01613 T00057    3    2.  AT  THE  TIME A BORROWER APPLIES FOR A REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN, A
2011S01613 T00058    4  FACILITATOR SHALL DISCLOSE TO SUCH BORROWER ON A DOCUMENT THAT IS  SEPA-
2011S01613 T00059    5  RATE FROM THE LOAN APPLICATION:
2011S01613 T00060    6    (A)  THE  ESTIMATED  FEE  FOR  PREPARING  AND ELECTRONICALLY FILING AN
2011S01613 T00061    7  INCOME TAX RETURN;
2011S01613 T00062    8    (B) THE REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN FEE SCHEDULE;
2011S01613 T00063    9    (C) THE ANNUAL PERCENTAGE RATE FOR THE LOAN;
2011S01613 T00064   10    (D) THE ESTIMATED TOTAL COST TO THE BORROWER FOR  UTILIZING  A  REFUND
2011S01613 T00065   11  ANTICIPATION LOAN;
2011S01613 T00066   12    (E)  THE ESTIMATED NUMBER OF DAYS WITHIN WHICH THE LOAN PROCEEDS SHALL
2011S01613 T00067   13  BE PAID TO THE BORROWER IF THE LOAN IS APPROVED;
2011S01613 T00068   14    (F) THE BORROWER IS RESPONSIBLE FOR REPAYMENT OF THE LOAN AND  RELATED
2011S01613 T00069   15  FEES IN THE EVENT THE INCOME TAX REFUND IS NOT PAID OR NOT PAID IN FULL;
2011S01613 T00070   16  AND
2011S01613 T00071   17    (G)  THE AVAILABILITY OF ELECTRONIC FILING OF THE INCOME TAX RETURN OF
2011S01613 T00072   18  THE BORROWER AND THE AVERAGE TIME  ANNOUNCED  BY  THE  INTERNAL  REVENUE
2011S01613 T00073   19  SERVICE  WITHIN WHICH THE BORROWER CAN EXPECT TO RECEIVE A REFUND IF THE
2011S01613 T00074   20  BORROWER'S RETURN IS ELECTRONICALLY FILED  AND  THE  BORROWER  DOES  NOT
2011S01613 T00075   21  OBTAIN A REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN.
2011S01613 T00076   22    3.  NO  REFUND  ANTICIPATION  LOAN SHALL BE MADE AT ANY LOCATION OTHER
2011S01613 T00077   23  THAN A LOCATION IN WHICH THE PRINCIPAL BUSINESS IS TAX PREPARATION.  ALL
2011S01613 T00078   24  DISCLOSURE  DOCUMENTS  REQUIRED BY SUBDIVISION TWO OF THIS SECTION SHALL
2011S01613 T00079   25  BE AVAILABLE IN ENGLISH, SPANISH AND IN ANY  OTHER  LANGUAGE  SPOKEN  BY
2011S01613 T00080   26  MORE  THAN  FIVE  PERCENT  OF  THE  POPULATION  IN  THE  VICINITY OF THE
2011S01613 T00081   27  FACILITATOR'S LOCATION.
2011S01613 T00082   28    4. NOTWITHSTANDING ANY OTHER PROVISION  OF  THE  BANKING  LAW  OR  THE
2011S01613 T00083   29  GENERAL  OBLIGATIONS  LAW,  THE  INTEREST RATE FOR A REFUND ANTICIPATION
2011S01613 T00084   30  LOAN SHALL NOT EXCEED (A) SIXTY PERCENT PER ANNUM FOR THE INITIAL  TWEN-
2011S01613 T00085   31  TY-ONE DAYS OF SUCH LOAN, AND (B) TWENTY PERCENT PER ANNUM FOR THE PERI-
2011S01613 T00086   32  OD  COMMENCING  ON  THE TWENTY-SECOND DAY OF SUCH LOAN AND ENDING ON THE
2011S01613 T00087   33  DATE OF PAYMENT.
2011S01613 T00088   34    5. ANY FACILITATOR WHO VIOLATES ANY PROVISION OF THIS SECTION SHALL BE
2011S01613 T00089   35  SUBJECT TO A CIVIL PENALTY OF NOT MORE THAN  FIVE  HUNDRED  DOLLARS  FOR
2011S01613 T00090   36  EACH  SUCH  VIOLATION. SUCH PENALTY SHALL BE ASSESSED BY THE SUPERINTEN-
2011S01613 T00091   37  DENT AS PROVIDED IN SECTION FORTY-FOUR OF THIS ARTICLE. IN ADDITION, ANY
2011S01613 T00092   38  FACILITATOR WHO VIOLATES ANY PROVISION OF THIS SECTION SHALL  BE  LIABLE
2011S01613 T00093   39  TO  ANY  AGGRIEVED BORROWER IN AN AMOUNT EQUAL TO THREE TIMES THE AMOUNT
2011S01613 T00094   40  OF THE REFUND ANTICIPATION LOAN FEE, PLUS REASONABLE ATTORNEY'S FEES, IN
2011S01613 T00095   41  A CIVIL ACTION BROUGHT BY THE AGGRIEVED  BORROWER  OR  BY  THE  ATTORNEY
2011S01613 T00096   42  GENERAL ON BEHALF OF THE AGGRIEVED BORROWER.
2011S01613 T00097   43    6.  THE  SUPERINTENDENT  MAY  PRESCRIBE  REGULATIONS  TO CARRY OUT THE
2011S01613 T00098   44  PROVISIONS AND PURPOSES OF THIS SECTION.
2011S01613 T00099   45    S 2. Nothing in this act shall be construed to  impair  or  limit  the
2011S01613 T00000.SO DOC S 1613                                   BTXT                 2011
2011S01613 T00100   46  validity  of  any additional local laws or regulations, not inconsistent
2011S01613 T00101   47  with the provisions of this act, applicable  to  the  making  of  refund
2011S01613 T00102   48  anticipation loans.
2011S01613 T00103   49    S  3.  If any clause, sentence, paragraph, section or part of this act
2011S01613 T00104   50  be adjudged by any court of competent jurisdiction to be  invalid,  such
2011S01613 T00105   51  judgment shall not affect, impair or invalidate the remainder hereof but

2011A01656 T00017
2011A01656 T00018       AN  ACT  to  amend the public authorities law, in relation to smart grid
2011A01656 T00019         systems
2011A01656 T00020
2011A01656 T00021         THE PEOPLE OF THE STATE OF NEW YORK, REPRESENTED IN SENATE AND  ASSEM-
2011A01656 T00022       BLY, DO ENACT AS FOLLOWS:
2011A01656 T00023
2011A01656 T00024    1    Section 1. The public authorities law is amended by adding a new title
2011A01656 T00025    2  13 to article 5 to read as follows:
2011A01656 T00026
2011A01656 T00027    3                                  TITLE 13
2011A01656 T00028    4                      NEW YORK STATE SMART GRID SYSTEMS
2011A01656 T00029
2011A01656 T00030    5  SECTION 1349-A. LEGISLATIVE INTENT.
2011A01656 T00031    6          1349-B. DEFINITIONS.
2011A01656 T00032    7          1349-C. RECOVERING COSTS.
2011A01656 T00033    8          1349-D. DEPLOYMENT PLAN.
2011A01656 T00034    9          1349-E. ECONOMIC INCENTIVES.
2011A01656 T00035   10          1349-F. INSTALLATION.
2011A01656 T00036   11          1349-G. ELECTRICAL CORPORATION.
2011A01656 T00037   12          1349-H. PROHIBITED REGULATION.
2011A01656 T00038
2011A01656 T00039   13    S  1349-A.  LEGISLATIVE INTENT. THE LEGISLATURE FINDS AND DECLARES ALL
2011A01656 T00040   14  OF THE FOLLOWING:
2011A01656 T00041   15    1. SMART GRID SYSTEMS THAT ALLOW REAL-TIME, TWO-WAY  DIGITAL  COMMUNI-
2011A01656 T00042   16  CATIONS  BETWEEN ELECTRIC UTILITIES AND THEIR DISTRIBUTION GRID AND WITH
2011A01656 T00043   17  THEIR CUSTOMERS CAN GREATLY IMPROVE THE EFFICIENCY  AND  RELIABILITY  OF
2011A01656 T00044   18  ELECTRICAL  DISTRIBUTION SYSTEMS AND FACILITATE CONSERVATION BY ENABLING
2011A01656 T00045   19  REAL-TIME DEMAND RESPONSE PRICING.
2011A01656 T00046   20    2. SMART GRID SYSTEMS  CONSTITUTE  CRITICAL  INFRASTRUCTURE  THAT  CAN
2011A01656 T00047   21  SUPPORT  IMPORTANT  HOMELAND  SECURITY NEEDS, BOTH BY PROVIDING DISASTER
2011A01656 T00048
2011A01656 T00049        EXPLANATION--Matter in ITALICS (underscored) is new; matter in brackets
2011A01656 T00050                             [ ] is old law to be omitted.
2011A01656 T00051                                                                  LBD04520-01-1
2011A01656 T00052
2011A01656 T00053       A. 1656                             2
2011A01656 T00054
2011A01656 T00055    1  PREVENTION AND RECOVERY CAPABILITIES TO  PROTECT  THE  STATE'S  ELECTRIC
2011A01656 T00056    2  GRID  AND BY ENABLING REMOTE MONITORING OF OTHER CRITICAL INFRASTRUCTURE
2011A01656 T00057    3  AND KEY ASSETS.
2011A01656 T00058    4    3.  SMART GRID SYSTEMS WILL PERMIT THE STATE TO TAKE FULL ADVANTAGE OF
2011A01656 T00059    5  DISTRIBUTED GENERATION RESOURCES THAT WILL INCREASE  DISTRIBUTION  EFFI-
2011A01656 T00060    6  CIENCY,   LOWER  CUSTOMER  PRICES,  STIMULATE  INNOVATION  AND  NEW  JOB
2011A01656 T00061    7  CREATION, AND  ULTIMATELY  REDUCE  EMISSIONS  OF  GREENHOUSE  GASES  AND
2011A01656 T00062    8  DECREASE DEPENDENCE ON FOREIGN OIL.
2011A01656 T00063    9    S 1349-B. DEFINITIONS. FOR PURPOSES OF THIS TITLE, THE FOLLOWING TERMS
2011A01656 T00064   10  HAVE THE FOLLOWING MEANINGS:
2011A01656 T00065   11    1. "ELECTRIC UTILITY" SHALL MEAN AN ELECTRICAL CORPORATION, ELECTRICAL
2011A01656 T00066   12  COOPERATIVE, OR LOCAL PUBLICLY OWNED ELECTRIC UTILITY.
2011A01656 T00067   13    2.  "ELECTRICAL  DELIVERY SYSTEM" SHALL MEAN THOSE FACILITIES THAT ARE
2011A01656 T00068   14  USED BY AN ELECTRICAL  CORPORATION,  ELECTRICAL  COOPERATIVE,  OR  LOCAL
2011A01656 T00069   15  PUBLICLY  OWNED  ELECTRIC UTILITY TO TRANSMIT, DELIVER, OR FURNISH ELEC-
2011A01656 T00070   16  TRICITY TO RETAIL END-USE CUSTOMERS.
2011A01656 T00071   17    3. "SMART GRID SYSTEM" SHALL MEAN A TWO-WAY COMMUNICATIONS SYSTEM  AND
2011A01656 T00072   18  ASSOCIATED  EQUIPMENT AND SOFTWARE, INCLUDING EQUIPMENT INSTALLED ON THE
2011A01656 T00073   19  ELECTRICAL DELIVERY SYSTEM AND ON THE PREMISES OF RETAIL END-USE CUSTOM-
2011A01656 T00074   20  ERS, THAT UTILIZES THE ELECTRICAL DELIVERY SYSTEM TO  PROVIDE  REAL-TIME
2011A01656 T00075   21  MONITORING,  DIAGNOSTIC,  AND  CONTROL  INFORMATION  AND  SERVICES  THAT
2011A01656 T00076   22  IMPROVE THE EFFICIENCY AND RELIABILITY OF THE DISTRIBUTION  AND  USE  OF
2011A01656 T00077   23  ELECTRICITY,  INCLUDING AUTOMATED LOAD CONTROL OR DEMAND RESPONSE, POWER
2011A01656 T00078   24  LOSS DETECTION AND PREVENTION, REMOTE OUTAGE AND RESTORATION  DETECTION,
2011A01656 T00079   25  CONTINUOUS  REPORTING OF UTILITY AND CUSTOMER DEMAND, DYNAMIC PRICING OF
2011A01656 T00080   26  ELECTRICAL SERVICE, PERFORMANCE MONITORING  OF  ELECTRICAL  DISTRIBUTION
2011A01656 T00081   27  NETWORK  EQUIPMENT, AND PREDICTIVE MAINTENANCE AND DIAGNOSTICS. AN ELEC-
2011A01656 T00082   28  TRIC UTILITY MAY TREAT AN ELECTRICAL METER INSTALLED TO ENABLE THE ELEC-
2011A01656 T00083   29  TRICAL DELIVERY SYSTEM TO FUNCTION PROPERLY AS BEING PART OF  THE  SMART
2011A01656 T00084   30  GRID  SYSTEM  IF THE METER HAS THE CAPABILITY OF MEASURING AND RECORDING
2011A01656 T00085   31  ELECTRICITY USAGE DATA  ON  A  TIME-DIFFERENTIATED  BASIS  OF  AT  LEAST
2011A01656 T00086   32  FIFTEEN  MINUTE  INTERVALS  FOR AT LEAST FOUR SEPARATE TIME SEGMENTS PER
2011A01656 T00087   33  DAY.
2011A01656 T00088   34    S 1349-C. RECOVERING COSTS. 1. IT  IS  THE  POLICY  OF  THE  STATE  TO
2011A01656 T00089   35  ENCOURAGE  AND, WHERE APPROPRIATE, MANDATE THE UTILIZATION OF SMART GRID
2011A01656 T00090   36  SYSTEMS BY ELECTRIC UTILITIES.
2011A01656 T00091   37    2. AN ELECTRIC UTILITY SHALL RECOVER ITS REASONABLE  COSTS  FOR  PLAN-
2011A01656 T00092   38  NING,  BUILDING,  AND  OPERATING  A  SMART  GRID SYSTEM FROM RATEPAYERS,
2011A01656 T00093   39  INCLUDING ADMINISTRATIVE  AND  OPERATIONAL  COSTS,  COSTS  FOR  SERVICES
2011A01656 T00094   40  RENDERED  BY UTILITY EMPLOYEES, CONTRACTORS, AND SUBCONTRACTORS, CAPITAL
2011A01656 T00095   41  INVESTMENT AND DEPRECIATION, TAXES, FINANCING, FINANCIAL INCENTIVES PAID
2011A01656 T00096   42  TO CUSTOMERS FOR PARTICIPATION IN DEMAND  RESPONSE,  LOAD  CONTROL,  AND
2011A01656 T00097   43  OTHER  CONSERVATION  PROGRAMS,  AND  MARKETING AND ADVERTISING COSTS FOR
2011A01656 T00098   44  SUCH PROGRAMS.
2011A01656 T00099   45    3. AN ELECTRIC UTILITY SHALL RECOVER THE REASONABLE COSTS OF EQUIPMENT
2011A01656 T00000.SO DOC A 1656                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01656 T00100   46  RENDERED OBSOLETE BY DEPLOYMENT OF A SMART GRID  SYSTEM,  BASED  ON  THE
2011A01656 T00101   47  REMAINING DEPRECIABLE LIFE OF THE OBSOLETE EQUIPMENT.
2011A01656 T00102   48    4.  AN  ELECTRIC  UTILITY  SHALL NOT RECOVER THE COSTS OF EQUIPMENT OR
2011A01656 T00103   49  SOFTWARE FROM RATEPAYERS UNLESS THE EQUIPMENT AND SOFTWARE IS COMPATIBLE
2011A01656 T00104   50  WITH, AND CAPABLE OF INTEROPERATING WITH, A SMART GRID SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00105   51    5. SUBDIVISION FOUR OF THIS SECTION DOES NOT APPLY  IN  THE  FOLLOWING
2011A01656 T00106   52  SITUATIONS:  (A) THE ELECTRIC UTILITY HAS, PRIOR TO FEBRUARY TWENTY-SEC-
2011A01656 T00107   53  OND, TWO THOUSAND EIGHT, ENTERED INTO A BINDING FINANCIAL COMMITMENT  TO
2011A01656 T00108   54  MAKE  A  PURCHASE OF, OR EXPENDITURE FOR, THE EQUIPMENT OR SOFTWARE THAT
2011A01656 T00109   55  IS NOT COMPATIBLE WITH, OR CAPABLE OF INTEROPERATING WITH, A SMART  GRID
2011A01656 T00110   56  SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00111
2011A01656 T00112       A. 1656                             3
2011A01656 T00113
2011A01656 T00114    1    (B)  THE EQUIPMENT OR SOFTWARE IS FOR PROVIDING SERVICE IN A GEOGRAPH-
2011A01656 T00115    2  ICAL AREA WHERE THE DEMONSTRATED COST OF DEPLOYING A SMART  GRID  SYSTEM
2011A01656 T00116    3  EXCEEDS  THE  REASONABLY  ANTICIPATED  BENEFITS OF DEPLOYMENT, INCLUDING
2011A01656 T00117    4  BENEFITS TO THE UTILITY, RATEPAYERS, THE ENVIRONMENT, AND HOMELAND SECU-
2011A01656 T00118    5  RITY.
2011A01656 T00119    6    S 1349-D. DEPLOYMENT PLAN. 1. EACH ELECTRIC UTILITY WITH MORE THAN TEN
2011A01656 T00120    7  THOUSAND SERVICE CONNECTIONS SHALL DEVELOP AND ADOPT A SMART GRID SYSTEM
2011A01656 T00121    8  DEPLOYMENT  PLAN  BY  JUNE  THIRTIETH,  TWO THOUSAND TWELVE. AN ELECTRIC
2011A01656 T00122    9  UTILITY WITH TEN THOUSAND OR FEWER  SERVICE  CONNECTIONS  MAY  ELECT  TO
2011A01656 T00123   10  DEVELOP AND ADOPT A SMART GRID SYSTEM DEPLOYMENT PLAN.
2011A01656 T00124   11    2.  EACH  ELECTRIC UTILITY SHALL, BY SEPTEMBER THIRTIETH, TWO THOUSAND
2011A01656 T00125   12  TWELVE, ISSUE A SMART GRID SYSTEM REQUEST FOR PROPOSALS CONSISTENT  WITH
2011A01656 T00126   13  THE  DEPLOYMENT  PLAN. RESPONDENTS TO A REQUEST FOR PROPOSAL SHALL OFFER
2011A01656 T00127   14  TO SERVE AT LEAST A MAJORITY OF THE ELECTRIC UTILITY'S RESIDENTIAL ELEC-
2011A01656 T00128   15  TRIC SUBSCRIBERS.
2011A01656 T00129   16    3. UNLESS SUBDIVISION FOUR OF THIS SECTION IS APPLICABLE, AN  ELECTRIC
2011A01656 T00130   17  UTILITY  SHALL MAKE A FINAL SELECTION OF A WINNING RESPONSE TO ITS SMART
2011A01656 T00131   18  GRID SYSTEM REQUEST FOR PROPOSALS NO LATER THAN ONE HUNDRED TWENTY  DAYS
2011A01656 T00132   19  AFTER THE DATE THE REQUEST FOR PROPOSALS IS ISSUED. ANY WINNING RESPONSE
2011A01656 T00133   20  SELECTED  SHALL  PROPOSE  TO CONSTRUCT A SMART GRID SYSTEM THAT PROVIDES
2011A01656 T00134   21  SUFFICIENT CAPACITY AND CAPABILITIES TO  MEET  ANTICIPATED  DEMANDS  FOR
2011A01656 T00135   22  MANAGEMENT  AND  CONTROL  OF  THE ELECTRIC UTILITY'S ELECTRICAL DELIVERY
2011A01656 T00136   23  SYSTEM UNTIL AT LEAST DECEMBER THIRTY-FIRST, TWO THOUSAND TWENTY-SIX.
2011A01656 T00137   24    4. AN ELECTRIC UTILITY MAY DECLINE TO SELECT A WINNING  PROPOSAL  ONLY
2011A01656 T00138   25  IF THERE ARE NO PROPOSALS MEETING THE REQUIREMENTS OF THE REQUEST OR THE
2011A01656 T00139   26  ELECTRIC  UTILITY MAKES WRITTEN FINDINGS THAT THE COSTS TO IMPLEMENT ANY
2011A01656 T00140   27  BIDS MEETING THE REQUIREMENTS OF THE PROPOSAL WOULD CLEARLY OUTWEIGH THE
2011A01656 T00141   28  POTENTIAL BENEFITS OF DEPLOYING A SMART GRID SYSTEM, INCLUDING  ENVIRON-
2011A01656 T00142   29  MENTAL  BENEFITS AND DIRECT AND INDIRECT BENEFITS TO THE UTILITY'S RATE-
2011A01656 T00143   30  PAYERS.
2011A01656 T00144   31    S 1349-E. ECONOMIC INCENTIVES. 1. BY APRIL FIRST, TWO THOUSAND TWELVE,
2011A01656 T00145   32  THE COMMISSION SHALL ESTABLISH RULES TO ENSURE  THAT  ELECTRICAL  CORPO-
2011A01656 T00146   33  RATIONS  WITH  MORE  THAN TEN THOUSAND SERVICE CONNECTIONS HAVE ADEQUATE
2011A01656 T00147   34  ECONOMIC INCENTIVES TO  DEPLOY  SMART  GRID  SYSTEMS.  THE  RULES  SHALL
2011A01656 T00148   35  ENCOURAGE ELECTRICAL CORPORATIONS TO DEPLOY SMART GRID SYSTEMS THAT HAVE
2011A01656 T00149   36  SUFFICIENT  CAPACITY AND CAPABILITIES TO MEET ANTICIPATED FUTURE DEMANDS
2011A01656 T00150   37  FOR MANAGEMENT AND CONTROL OF THE ELECTRICAL DISTRIBUTION  SYSTEM  UNTIL
2011A01656 T00151   38  AT  LEAST  DECEMBER  THIRTY-FIRST, TWO THOUSAND TWENTY-SIX. THE ECONOMIC
2011A01656 T00152   39  INCENTIVES SHALL, FOR SMART GRID SYSTEMS DEPLOYED ON OR  AFTER  DECEMBER
2011A01656 T00153   40  THIRTY-FIRST, TWO THOUSAND EIGHT, INCLUDE ONE OR MORE OF THE FOLLOWING:
2011A01656 T00154   41    (A) AN ENHANCED RETURN ON ITS REASONABLE CAPITAL EXPENDITURES AND ON A
2011A01656 T00155   42  PORTION  OF  ITS REASONABLE OPERATIONS AND MAINTENANCE COSTS FOR A SMART
2011A01656 T00156   43  GRID SYSTEM; OR
2011A01656 T00157   44    (B) RETENTION OF A PORTION OF ANY COST SAVINGS ATTRIBUTABLE TO THE USE
2011A01656 T00158   45  OF A SMART GRID SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00159   46    2. THE GOVERNING BOARD OF AN ELECTRIC UTILITY THAT  IS  NOT  AN  ELEC-
2011A01656 T00160   47  TRICAL CORPORATION MAY ESTABLISH INCENTIVES TO DEPLOY SMART GRID SYSTEMS
2011A01656 T00161   48  CONSISTENT WITH SUBDIVISION ONE OF THIS SECTION.
2011A01656 T00162   49    3.  AN  ELECTRICAL  CORPORATION  WITH  TEN  THOUSAND  OR FEWER SERVICE
2011A01656 T00163   50  CONNECTIONS MAY FILE AN APPLICATION WITH THE COMMISSION SEEKING AUTHORI-
2011A01656 T00164   51  ZATION TO ESTABLISH INCENTIVES TO DEPLOY SMART GRID  SYSTEMS  CONSISTENT
2011A01656 T00165   52  WITH SUBDIVISION ONE OF THIS SECTION.
2011A01656 T00166   53    S  1349-F.  INSTALLATION.  1.  AN  ELECTRIC UTILITY OR ITS CONTRACTORS
2011A01656 T00167   54  INSTALLING A SMART GRID SYSTEM SHALL BE PERMITTED ACCESS TO  ANY  POLES,
2011A01656 T00168   55  DUCTS,  CONDUITS,  AND RIGHTS-OF-WAY ON TERMS AND CONDITIONS AT LEAST AS
2011A01656 T00169
2011A01656 T00170       A. 1656                             4
2011A01656 T00171
2011A01656 T00172    1  FAVORABLE AS THOSE GRANTED TO A HOLDER OF A STATE FRANCHISE. THE  RIGHTS
2011A01656 T00173    2  GRANTED BY THIS SECTION DO NOT LIMIT EITHER OF THE FOLLOWING:
2011A01656 T00174    3    (A)  ANY  RIGHT  THAT A UTILITY OR THIRD PARTY INSTALLING A SMART GRID
2011A01656 T00175    4  SYSTEM MAY HAVE TO ACCESS  POLES,  DUCTS,  CONDUITS,  AND  RIGHTS-OF-WAY
2011A01656 T00176    5  PURSUANT TO CONTRACT OR UNDER ANY OTHER LAW; OR
2011A01656 T00177    6    (B) THE SERVICES THAT MAY BE OFFERED OVER A SMART GRID SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00178    7    2.  A  SMART  GRID  SYSTEM  IS AN INTEGRAL COMPONENT OF THE ELECTRICAL
2011A01656 T00179    8  DELIVERY SYSTEM AND THE INSTALLATION OF A SMART GRID  SYSTEM  SHALL  NOT
2011A01656 T00180    9  REQUIRE  AN ELECTRIC UTILITY OR ITS CONTRACTOR TO OBTAIN OR EXPAND EASE-
2011A01656 T00181   10  MENTS OR OTHER RIGHTS-OF-WAY OR TO PROVIDE ADDITIONAL CONSIDERATION AS A
2011A01656 T00182   11  RESULT OF THE INSTALLATION  OR  OPERATION  OF  THE  SMART  GRID  SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00183   12  INSTALLATION OF A SMART GRID SYSTEM IS CONSISTENT WITH, AND PART OF, THE
2011A01656 T00184   13  INSTALLATION OF THE ELECTRICAL DISTRIBUTION SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00185   14    S  1349-G. ELECTRICAL CORPORATION. AN ELECTRICAL CORPORATION MAY ELECT
2011A01656 T00186   15  TO OWN AND OPERATE A SMART GRID SYSTEM ON ITS  OWN  ELECTRICAL  DELIVERY
2011A01656 T00187   16  SYSTEM,  OR  MAY  PERMIT  AN AFFILIATED OR UNAFFILIATED ENTITY TO OWN OR
2011A01656 T00188   17  OPERATE THE SMART GRID SYSTEM.
2011A01656 T00189   18    S 1349-H.  PROHIBITED  REGULATION.  A  LOCAL  MUNICIPALITY  SHALL  NOT
2011A01656 T00190   19  PROHIBIT OR REGULATE EITHER OF THE FOLLOWING:
2011A01656 T00191   20    (A)  THE  INSTALLATION OR OPERATION OF A SMART GRID SYSTEM BY AN ELEC-
2011A01656 T00192   21  TRICAL CORPORATION OR ELECTRICAL COOPERATIVE, OR A CONTRACTOR OR  AFFIL-
2011A01656 T00193   22  IATE,  WITHIN  THE  SERVICE  AREA OF THE ELECTRICAL CORPORATION OR ELEC-
2011A01656 T00194   23  TRICAL COOPERATIVE; OR
2011A01656 T00195   24    (B) THE INSTALLATION OR OPERATION OF A SMART GRID SYSTEM  BY  A  LOCAL
2011A01656 T00196   25  PUBLICLY  OWNED  ELECTRIC  UTILITY,  OR A CONTRACTOR, WITHIN THE SERVICE
2011A01656 T00197   26  AREA OF THE UTILITY, WHEN APPROVED BY THE GOVERNING BOARD OF THE  UTILI-
2011A01656 T00198   27  TY.
2011A01656 T00000.SO DOC A 1656                                   BTXT                 2011
2011A01656 T00199   28    S 2. This act shall take effect on the one hundred twentieth day after
2011A01656 T00200   29  it shall have become a law; provided, however, that effective immediate-
2011A01656 T00201   30  ly,  the  addition,  amendment  and/or  repeal of any rule or regulation
2011A01656 T00202   31  necessary for the implementation of this act on its effective  date  are
2011A01656 T00203   32  authorized  and  directed  to  be  made  and completed on or before such
2011A01656 T00204   33  effective date.
